Free Talk

Reflections on the Tortoiseshell Beam

— Swallow

The Japanese archipelago of the three islands of Nie Er, always harboring the arrogance of a rustic bumpkin. The people of that country value martial prowess, and call themselves "Great Harmony." They implicitly establish the country on the way of the warrior, seeking to take the lead in Eastern martial arts. In reality, in the art of boxing, they only have a superficial understanding. They are not proficient in either the Shaolin or Wudang schools, let alone the internal energy of breathing exercises. However, the Japanese swords produced in that country have a sharpness that can cut iron like mud. However, they are far inferior to the Miao saber, which is flexible enough to wrap around paper. Twenty years ago, Yan Ren Huo Yuanjia came to Shanghai to perform and display his skills, and his courage was known throughout China and abroad. A certain Japanese samurai, who claimed to be the best fighter in his country, wanted to compete with Huo on stage. Huo feared that injuring the samurai would cause diplomatic trouble, and firmly refused. The samurai suspected Huo of being cowardly and exaggerated his claims in various newspapers, even accusing Huo of being falsely renowned. Huo's disciples were numerous, and the young and spirited were indignant. They secretly competed with the samurai, but were defeated. As a result, the samurai's arrogance increased. He personally knocked on Huo's door, insisting on a trial. Huo smiled and said, "Forced into this situation, don't blame me for being reckless. Why not first test our hand strength?" The samurai readily agreed, saying, "Everything is fate." Proud and full of spirit, he stretched out his hands and forcefully attacked Huo. Huo raised his palms to meet him. As soon as they made contact, the samurai fell several feet away. Huo stepped forward and smiled to comfort him. The samurai was extremely ashamed and sweating profusely, knowing that he was no match for Huo's strength. He changed his demeanor and thanked Huo, offering to become his disciple. His attitude was quite respectful. Huo was naturally chivalrous and did not take it to heart. Little did he know that the samurai had already harbored the intention to kill Huo. The samurai formally took the disciple's oath, and Huo meticulously taught him, and his skills advanced rapidly. The following year, the samurai invited Huo to the East to interact with the way of the warrior in his country, secretly placing a slow-acting poison in the wine. Huo, unaware, drank it heartily. Before long, he fell ill. The samurai pretended to be concerned and immediately sent him to the hospital. The doctor was also influenced by the samurai's machinations, and the treatment made him more and more seriously ill. By the time he returned to China, the illness was incurable. A great hero was actually plotted against by a Japanese slave. Writing this, I can't help but feel tears welling up in my eyes. I throw down my pen and wail loudly. Alas, Huo Yuanjia.

Don't Remove the Court Grass Studio Husband's Anecdotes

Dialogue Before the God of War (3)

"Although success or failure is debatable, how can survival or demise be ignored? Losing the country means becoming a slave of the conquered, which should be considered."

"There are distinctions among those who lose their country. Those who lose their country without a fight are called slaves of the conquered. Those who are defeated repeatedly, fighting again and again, and still inevitably lose their country to others are righteous people, and the country of righteous people is called a righteous country. Righteousness lasts forever, who can destroy it? Who can enslave it? During the European War, wasn't Belgium occupied for a time? But no one called the Belgians slaves of the conquered. Why? The Belgians had already fought to the death to defend their neutrality and maintain their national character. Besides white people, America also has black and red people. Black people were once called black slaves, and their bodies could be bought and sold, lacking the spirit of struggle. The red people are a nation that cannot be subdued by force, preferring death to surrender. Although the red race is gradually dwindling, there is not a single red slave. White people with black ancestors are often looked down upon, while those with red ancestors are respected. We don't need to fear losing the country! Losing without a fight is the greatest shame in the world."

"What you say is true, but China's internal disunity makes me feel uneasy."

"Have the Chinese people ever been disunited? Have they ever not been united against foreign aggression? It is only the politicians and warlords who are disunited. Unity cannot be achieved by empty talk. Declaring war on the violent Japanese for the sake of justice and humanity will naturally lead to unity."

Small Tribe in Tainan Determined to Resist Japan

— Rooster Crest

An old friend, Mr. Wang Yanan, once traveled to Japan and visited various islands in the South Seas. He mentioned that in Taiwan, there is a village called Guangcun, located in the mountains. The indigenous people living in the village do not interact with the Japanese. Their tradition of resisting Japan has been steadfastly maintained for generations. This is also a matter worthy of attention.

The so-called Guangcun is the indigenous pronunciation. The area is located in the mountains of Tainan, and is a settlement of a type of Taiwanese aborigines. The population is only a few dozen families. They marry among themselves and do not interact with outsiders. They are skilled in martial arts, and climbing mountains and crossing ridges is a common skill. Even women can chase birds and are as strong as men. Currently, these aborigines still farm and weave themselves and refuse to be assimilated by the Japanese. Their spirit of resisting Japan is admirable.

It is said that more than ten years ago, a Japanese garrison commander named Fukushima often liked to go on exploratory tours during his military leisure time. One day, he arrived at the village and was surrounded and attacked by the aborigines. Three guards died. Fukushima escaped and fled, then led troops to suppress them. However, the mountains were empty, and there was no trace of anyone. Unable to search, he returned in disappointment. Afterwards, he repeatedly sent scouts to investigate, but there was little news. In fact, the aborigines moved around and had no fixed whereabouts, so the Japanese were helpless. In recent years, the Japanese population has been sparse and not a cause for concern, so they have been allowed to live and die on their own without interference. Therefore, when the people of Tainan mention Guangcun, they treat it as outside of civilization.

It is also said that the residents of Guangcun are indeed one of the oldest indigenous groups in Tainan. When the Japanese seized Taiwan, their chieftain once vowed to resist Japan. He was killed for his resistance. Now, his descendants live in the mountains, and their hatred for Japan has not diminished at all. Small tribes have never lacked ambition and are worthy of emulation.

World Small News

It is becoming popular in the United States to trade goods instead of using money. Country doctors treat patients without charging fees, instead accepting chickens and eggs as payment. Farming tools can also be purchased without money, using wheat as collateral. One school does not charge students tuition, instead accepting wheat.

The town of Saga in the Prussian province of Silesia produces a large number of cats. Therefore, families that keep cats must pay taxes. Each family pays one pound for one cat, three pounds for the second cat, and four pounds for four cats.

Canada's fur trade has become a major industry, worth six million pounds annually. There are 5,513 fur factories that produce mink, fox, otter, muskrat, and water mink fur for people to keep warm.

The British man Bunyan's immortal work "Pilgrim's Progress" still sells very well, having been translated into 126 languages, breaking all literary records.

The Rheims region of France produces the most grapes. This year, due to pests and bad weather, the harvest is very small. It is said that there will be no new ingredients for making champagne after 1931.

A White Sparrow

— Shallow

My friend Pan Zian mentioned yesterday that a strange sparrow was found near his home. Its appearance is no different from ordinary sparrows, except that its feathers are pure white. It is capricious and difficult to catch. It took more than twenty days of effort to put it in a cage. He once checked the Compendium of Materia Medica, but there was no mention of its use, but it was said to be an auspicious sign. I don't know if the bird is truly rare and precious, or if it is a white pig from Liaodong. Therefore, I publish it in the newspaper to inquire about the world's knowledgeable people.

Talking About Milk in Early Winter

— Ms. Yeh Hua

The suffering of mankind due to improper diet has only gradually been resolved. At the end of the nineteenth century, the dawn of organic chemical knowledge appeared. Food was analyzed into simple chemical compounds. In the last twenty years, the principle of nutrition was discovered, and the value of milk increased tenfold. As a result, the dairy industry has transformed from family-run businesses into enterprises with capital of one or two million yuan. The commercial sale of dairy products has also emerged. The problem is becoming more complex. Those that are related to us, I write on the left.

Dairy cows and milk All cows that can produce milk for a long time, and the price of milk is higher than the price of meat, are called dairy cows. Their ancestor was Bos. The Bos family is the same as other cows. Dairy cows are improved by breeding. There are two types of cattle. One is Bos indicus, and the other is Bos taurus. Artificial breeding methods were then used to increase the number of species. The excellent dairy cows are Jersey, Guernsey, and Holstein. The Jersey color ranges from light gray to dark gray jujube red tea. The average weight per head is 900 pounds. It produces about 19 pounds of milk per day. Rich in butterfat. The oil globules are very large. The Guernsey has various colors of white, yellow, and red. Light ones weigh 1,000 pounds and heavy ones weigh 1,300 pounds. It can produce 22 pounds of milk per day. The pigment is uniquely rich. Other cows cannot match it. It can attract customers. Dairy farms are happy to use it. Holstein milk production is second to none among cows. It contains less oil. The color is whiter. It has more protein. It is most suitable for feeding children. This cow has black and white spots. Its weight is 1,700 pounds. It is the largest of the cattle. We should pay attention to three things when drinking milk.

Microbes and milk Milk can nourish people, and it can also nourish microbes. In healthy cows, every cubic centimeter of milk has hundreds of microbes at most, and only ten or so at least. Harding found an average of 428 microbes per cubic centimeter in 1,230 samples of cow's milk. The temperature is especially high. The microbial productivity is especially fast. When milk is acidified, bacteria account for 90 percent. After the milk hardens, the bacteria reach 99 percent. Pulmonary tuberculosis, swollen hands and feet, typhoid fever,

Taiwanese Reporter's Hatred of Losing the Country (Part 2)

— Ms. Yeh Hua

News monopoly Since Taiwan fell into the hands of the Japanese, it has been isolated from the world. Letters and telegrams cannot be freely sent and received. The only source of foreign news in newspapers is the Japanese Electric News Agency and the United News Agency. The former is operated by Japanese sole proprietorship, and the latter is jointly operated by Japan and the United States. There are no other institutions besides these. Even Reuters manuscripts are banned. This is how the Taiwanese people are deceived. The world situation and human life are beyond their imagination. The Taiwanese newspapers are instructed to publicize the atrocities of the Japanese army in China, claiming that Chinese soldiers are all bandits, bullying small ethnic groups, harming the righteous Japanese army, and destroying Japan's vested interests in the eastern provinces. Such blood-curdling words that slander international morality, reversing right and wrong, and confusing black and white. Taiwanese people with knowledge know that they are being deceived, but they are trapped in a fog, and the truth is unknown.

The pain of inspection The Japanese have already seized Taiwanese newspapers, but they are still afraid of losing their news policy. They also conduct strict surveillance. The newspapers' layouts are sent to the police station for inspection before printing, called "review." On average, a blank space is seen every two or three days. Temporary suspensions and delayed printing occur several times a month. Reporters being fined, arrested, exiled, and missing are common. If a reporter has any anti-Japanese suspicion, plainclothes police will track them everywhere. They are inseparable from teahouses, pubs, street corners, and alleys. There is always the danger of family ruin and death. Compared to the infamous secret agents of Russia and the Italian Black Shirts, they are even more violent and reckless. Mr. Zhang said this with tears in his voice.

Diphtheria, rubella, sore throat, and gastrointestinal diseases are often mediated by milk bacteria. How can we not be afraid? In addition to cleaning the milk parlor, using small-mouthed milk buckets, and washing milking machines, the defensive method is to use Pasteur's sterilization method. This method raises the temperature of milk to over 160 degrees Fahrenheit for half a minute and then rapidly cools the temperature of the milk. This method is mostly used in large sea dairy farms. In recent years, there has been a method of disinfecting in bottles, so that the milk does not come into contact with the space again after disinfection. Borden invented canned milk in 1853. Substitutes for milk powder were invented by Custer, Campbell, and Sankeb, and were also disinfected.

Donating Paintings to Help the Black Army

— Ma Mengrong

The Japanese pirates are deepening day by day. The eastern corner has been lost. But the officials in power are calm and do not resist, sitting by and watching the humiliating loss of teachers and land. There is nothing that can be done. Only General Ma Zhanshan, with a small force, resisted tens of thousands of troops and became a pillar of the country. He supported half of the country and fought bloody battles. He repeatedly frustrated the enemy's offensive, and finally ran out of ammunition and had no reinforcements. He temporarily retreated to Hailun. When the alarm came, people here were all filled with hot anger. They competed to donate money to reward his soldiers. It is a true act of righteousness. Mr. Xu Xixi, the son-in-law of Mr. Wu Daiqiu of Shimen, is known for his calligraphy and painting. His clear and elegant style has long been famous in the art world. He came to Shanghai from Yuanhu. Mr. Wu Zhenping and Mr. Zhang Yisheng visited him at his residence. Mr. Xu said with emotion: "The country is in trouble. We scholars cannot throw our pens and join the army, or ride horses and kill thieves. I have been working with pens and ink for a long time. I have a hundred paintings in my chest. I am willing to sell them all and donate the money to the Black Army. The two gentlemen were inspired by his master. Mr. Zhang also donated dozens of his recent works. Mr. Wu prepared the event for him. The exhibition was held in the auditorium of the New World Hotel for three days starting on the 27th. I was in a hurry when I received Mr. Daiqiu's invitation, and Mr. Zhenping also asked me to attend. So I went to see it in the rain. Mr. Xu led me to read the works. I saw that his landscapes were thick and simple, with the method of the former sages, and no vulgar habits of the time. It was like his father-in-law's style. His inscriptions were also very similar. I know that he has gained a lot from Dai Weng. His imitations of Tang Liuru and Shen Shitian are also profound and upright. They are considered to be cooperative works. His flowers and plants are also outstanding in pen and ink, and his style is elegant. He has the strengths of Huishu, Menglu, and Zixiang. Xixi must have secretly studied the elders of Yuanhu. Yisheng is engaged in pattern painting and has recently devoted himself to traditional Chinese painting. He has also visited Dai Weng's gate. Therefore, his paintings also have Dai Weng's style. Dai Weng's landscape paintings are exquisite and highly valued in Jilin. The society has a fixed evaluation. I especially love his ancient and simple flowers and plants. I have not done landscape paintings for a long time. In recent years, I have been happy to write life to entertain myself. Dai Weng Xu is a work that has both ancient methods and new interests. He is a work that combines talent and hard work. He also encouraged me to make a book of flowers, birds, and insects as a model for painting learners. I am ashamed. (Move reward for black)

Rotary Club of Storytellers

Country Folks Arrive in Shanghai Again (34)

— Bao Tianxiao

At this time, the country folk seemed to be going crazy. People didn't know what he was doing? They couldn't pull him back. They thought he was a drunken man, but the country folk hadn't drunk any wine just now. They thought he was a crazy madman, but the country folk were not crazy. Passersby felt puzzled, and were afraid that he would cause some trouble, and everyone surrounded him and asked him what was wrong?

"Didn't you see what two words are on his electric light?"

Passersby, pointed out by the country folk, really raised their heads and opened their eyes to look at the electric lights above, and there was nothing strange about them, but they didn't know what he meant in his heart? Everyone just stared at him, hoping that he would explain in more detail.

"Do you know who the contemporary heroes of our country are?" The country folk said this very generously and excitedly among the many crowds.

Everyone was even more stunned when they heard this. They thought, could this country bumpkin really have a mental illness? Otherwise, he would have been poisoned by the newly popular martial arts novels. What heroes? What heroes? It's a mess. Probably, crazy people are talking about those kinds of gods and heroes, worshiping ancient heroes. Just like those who suffer from erotic mania, they are all eagerly admiring Cui Yingying in the Romance of the West Chamber and Lin Daiyu in Dream of the Red Chamber. Everyone also wanted to ignore the heroes asked by the country folk. And for a while, they couldn't answer who the heroes of the world are?

"Now in the era, can General Ma Zhanshan, the chairman of Heilongjiang, who is fighting hard in the frontier, be considered a contemporary hero of our country?"

As soon as the country folk said this, everyone agreed. In the agreement, there were also those who clapped their hands and cheered, saying:

"Hero! Hero! He is indeed a contemporary hero!" Everyone never thought that this country folk would be a patriot, and they all agreed that what he said was correct.

"Then do you all support General Ma Zhanshan?" The country folk had an attitude of leading the masses.

"Support General Ma Zhanshan!" "Support General Ma Zhanshan who is fighting hard in the frontier!"

At this time, the general public shouted slogans. The heroic situation inspired many pedestrians and gradually joined in.

"Since we all support General Ma Zhanshan, then if someone opposes General Ma Zhanshan, shouldn't we overthrow him? Look! Why is the electric light here marked with the two words "Anti-Occupy"? Isn't this clearly opposing Ma Zhanshan? Opposing Ma Zhanshan, shouldn't we unanimously protest?"

Breaking Through the 700 Tael Barrier The Bidding Gold Suddenly Plunged Again Yesterday, the situation was stable, and there were no special changes. Only after breaking through 700 taels, there were always a total of ten taels in retrospect. The total decline was more than five taels. Although the silver price fell, the big bars fell slightly, and they did not think so. Especially since the current situation is not very optimistic, the opening was low. In the future, advances and retreats often have three or four tael ranges. Each firm had no large ticket transactions. As for the foreign exchange trends, they differed. British pine and American firm were squeezing small exchanges. At noon, it once returned 700 taels. The market trend was loose and discounted, and a setback was seen again. The exchange rate turned out to be short. It is estimated that British gold can be purchased at one shilling and ten pence and a half, and US dollars at about twelve yuan. The gold price fell again by five or six taels, and people's hearts weakened again.

Morning Opened and Fell, Noon Recovered Slightly It opened one or two cents lower in the morning, at 699 taels. The gray market once traded at 701 taels. The big bars fell by five-sixteenths to three-eighths. The silver price decreased by a small cent, and the private telegram fell by six-eighths. Then it added to 701 taels, falling shortly after, because Hengyu, Yuanda Yong, Yuankangxiang, Hengchangyong, Bingxing, etc. all sold. Moreover, British gold was seen to be loosening, and the recent settlement was ten pence three-seven-five. Therefore, the gold price gradually fell, falling by ten taels, to ninety-one taels and five cents. Not long after, Guangdong Gang, Yifeng, and Cuichangyong bought in, and immediately raised it by four taels. Moreover, HSBC absorbed March British gold three-seven-five, and the Japanese Commercial Bank mutually did March US dollars thirty-one yuan eight-seven-five, resulting in ninety-five and a half taels. Moreover, British gold hung half a penny long, while US dollars shrunk three-seven-five, at ninety-three to four taels at the time. HSBC absorbed British gold three-seven-five again, slightly adding one or two taels, at ninety-five taels. Dadecheng and others sold out, immediately retreating two taels to ninety-three taels. HSBC offered ten pence three-one-two-five. After entering, Yuanmaoyong, Yuanda Yong, Yuanheng, Yifengyong, Yifeng, Tongtaichang, etc. all entered. Wanxing, Shunli, and Dalian Gang also slightly intervened. After only twenty minutes, it was pulled up by five taels, to ninety-eight taels when it was nearly ten o'clock. Later, due to retail investors and hedgers selling, and because US dollars in January could be traded in and out at thirty-two yuan, it was ninety-two and a half taels at ten twenty. Then there was a swing of three or four taels. After eleven o'clock, it was seen to rise again. After a while, the buying and selling were uneven, and people's hearts seemed to be going down. So it fell again by about two taels, to ninety-four taels and one cent. Then it added to ninety-five taels. When the market closed at four thirty, it was ninety-four taels and seven cents, falling again by five and a half taels compared to the previous day. Currency Exchange: Sterling Weak, Dollar Tight

Yesterday, the exchange rates for British pounds, American dollars, Indian rupees, and silver all fell. However, the exchange rate between British pounds and American dollars continued to decrease slightly. Consequently, the trend in the Shanghai market diverged significantly. HSBC's listed prices extended by two points, with British gold at half a penny, equivalent to one shilling, nine pence, and seventy-five farthings. American dollars, on the other hand, contracted by three seventy-fifths, equivalent to thirty yuan and six hundred twenty-five ten-thousandths. Hong Kong added one hundred twenty-five ten-thousandths, totaling seventy-six taels and six hundred eighty-seven and a half ten-thousandths. Indian rupees also weakened, while French and German currencies tightened. It seems the internal market for banks also reflected this trend, with sterling weak and the dollar tight. This was likely a move to squeeze small exchange rates. The market was initially chaotic and unpredictable in the early morning, but later eased and stabilized. It then turned unfavorable in the afternoon as the gold market suddenly returned to the 700 tael threshold. This was due to a slight drop in the London silver market, largely because the current situation remained chaotic, causing anxiety. As a result, compared to the day before, British gold rose by slightly more than one penny, while American dollars only increased by twenty-five ten-thousandths. Foreign Interest Eases Slightly, Silver Call Loans Remain Tight

As for the long-term tightness of silver supply, there was still no hope for easing. Although foreign interest rates fell yesterday, silver call loan rates remained firm. It is apparent that there is unlikely to be any turnaround in the current silver supply situation.

Government Bonds Continue to Rise by About Two Yuan

Market Trends Slightly Stable, Market Activity Strong

Yesterday (December 1st), the various bond market conditions on the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange saw a variety of spot transactions opening, and buying and selling were considered active. Although the futures market was strong, sales transactions were limited. Each bond still had a small amount of large transactions. At the beginning of the morning opening, due to good market sentiment, scattered purchases were active, and each bond rose sharply compared to when the market was suspended. There was also no major difference from the off-market trading the day before. However, as the market closed, market sentiment turned soft. The buying situation was not as enthusiastic as before, because the diplomatic situation was not as optimistic as the day before. The Japanese side had not repented of its wrongdoing, and its conspiracy to disturb was still in progress, while the League of Nations stood idly by, and there was still no way to mediate. Because of this, buying enthusiasm gradually declined, and each price fell back. In the later market, the trend was stable, hovering without great ups and downs. However, the closing situation and market sentiment were generally good. As a result, compared to the previous spot price, only the 1920 Goodness bond fell by more than three yuan compared to the middle of last month. The rest rose sharply. Only the disbandment 96 futures fell back. The rest continued to rise by more than one yuan or several jiao to more than two yuan. Yesterday's flour market, after the opening in the morning, the market for each month once presented a brisk image. After the opening, both near and far periods rose by 20 to 30 fen or so from the end of the previous month. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, the gold price had still returned to within the 700 tael mark, and the market situation was not as optimistic as expected. People's hearts became depressed again, and the sales of downstream products must be strong to stabilize. As a result, this month was 5 li better than the end of the previous month, January was 2.5 li better, February was 5 li better, March was 2.5 li better, April was 7.5 li better, and May was 1.5 fen lower than the opening price.

Wheat Market Turns Weak in the Afternoon

Yesterday's futures wheat market generally presented a stable image. Since foreign wheat quotations rebounded by about 60 or 70 jiao, and the market situation was slightly eased, after the opening, both near and far periods rose by 50 or 60 fen compared to the closing price of the previous month. Local News

Yesterday

Seven Types of Public Bonds Drawn by Lottery

Construction Bonds...Total Repayment of Principal and Interest: 370,000

Ministry of Finance's Six Types of Principal Repayment: 8,385,000

The Electrical Enterprise Long-Term and Short-Term Public Bonds of the National Government's Construction Committee held their second lottery for principal repayment at the Bankers Association at 11:00 AM yesterday. At 2:00 PM, the Ministry of Finance's Seventh Year, Six Percent Public Bonds held their eighth lottery for principal repayment, the Fourth Lottery for Principal Repayment of the Austrian Indemnity Guarantee 24 Treasury Bonds, the Sixth Lottery for Principal Repayment of Military Supplies Public Bonds, the Seventh Lottery for Principal Repayment of Post-War Short-Term Public Bonds, the Sixth Lottery for Principal Repayment of the Eighteenth Year Disaster Relief Public Bonds, and the Fourth Lottery for Principal Repayment of the Nineteenth Year Customs Tariff Public Bonds were all held simultaneously at the Bankers Association. The lottery situation for each type of public bond is recorded below.

Construction Bonds Lottery in the Morning

Lottery Situation: At 11:00 AM yesterday, when the Construction Bonds lottery was held, the attendees included Tseng Yang-fu, Vice Chairman of the National Government's Construction Committee; Wang Yan-song, from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Hsu Chi-ching, from the Bankers Association; Yen Chun-an, from the Money Dealers Association; Lin Kang-hou, Firestone Liang, Fan Chieh-tang, members of the Fund Custody Committee; Li Ti-sheng, from the Central Bank; Chu Chien-ming, from the Bank of China; Yen Yi-fu, from the Bank of Communications; Tian Chu, representing the Audit Council; and He Hsiao-chuan, representing the Ministry of Finance. Tseng Yang-fu presided over the event. Representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers Association, and the Ministry of Finance's Audit Council supervised the lottery. Representatives from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications executed the lottery.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Tseng Yang-fu reported that in 1930, the Construction Committee issued long-term public bonds for 1.5 million yuan at an annual interest rate of 6% because it took over the Chishuyan Electrical Plant. In order to expand the Capital Electrical Plant and the Chishuyan Electrical Plant, it also issued short-term public bonds for 2.5 million yuan at an annual interest rate of 8%. The first principal repayment was in June of this year. Today is the second principal repayment lottery. Four 6% long-term public bonds will be drawn, with a principal amount of 60,000 yuan and interest of 43,650 yuan. Seven 8% short-term public bonds will be drawn, with a principal amount of 175,000 yuan and interest of 93,000 yuan, for a total of 371,650 yuan.

Winning Numbers: The results of the lottery showed that the winning numbers for the four 6% long-term public bonds were 8, 53, 72, and 81. The winning numbers for the seven 8% short-term public bonds were 7, 19, 24, 33, 54, 67, and 79. Holders of the above winning numbers can collect their principal and interest from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications.

Afternoon Public Bond Lottery (Six Types)

Lottery Situation: At 2 PM, the Ministry of Finance held a lottery for six types of public bonds. Those present included: Zheng Lai, Director of the Ministry of Finance's Public Bond Department; Wang Xiaolai from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Yan Junan from the Silver Industry Association; Bei Songsun from the Banking Association; Wang Fang from the Auditing Yuan; Li Tisheng from the Central Bank; Wei Bo from the Bank of Communications; Cheng Muhao from the Bank of China; and Managing Committee members Pang Zeen and He Xiaojuan. The chairman was Song Ziwen (represented by Zheng Lai). Supervisors included four representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Silver and Money Industry Association, and the Auditing Yuan. Representatives from the China, Central, and Communications Banks executed the lottery.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Song Ziwen, representing Zheng Lai, Director of the Public Bond Department, delivered a speech, saying, "Today is the day for the principal redemption lottery for six types of bonds, including the 6% Public Bonds of the 7th Year of the Republic. I am delighted that you have all come to observe. Now, I will briefly report to you on the circumstances of each type of public bond: (1) The 6% Public Bonds of the 7th Year of the Republic had a total issuance of 45 million yuan. Since the 17th year of the Republic, they have been redeemed in 20 installments over 10 years. Seven installments have already been redeemed. This is the eighth installment, with a lottery of five tickets and a principal redemption of 2.25 million yuan. (2) The Austro-Hungarian Indemnity Secured 24 Treasury Bonds were issued in the 15th year of the Republic, with a total of 2.4 million yuan. Three installments have already been redeemed. This is the fourth installment, with a lottery of five tickets and a principal redemption of 120,000 yuan. (3) The National Government Ministry of Finance Military Needs Public Bonds were issued in the 17th year of the Republic, with a total of 10 million yuan. Since the 18th year of the Republic, they have been redeemed twice annually, with each redemption being one-twentieth of the total amount. Five installments have already been redeemed. This is the sixth installment, with a lottery of five tickets and a principal redemption of approximately 515,000 yuan. (4) The National Government Ministry of Finance Rehabilitation Short-Term Public Bonds were also issued in the 17th year of the Republic, with a total of 40 million yuan. Since the second half of the 17th year of the Republic, they have been redeemed in ten installments over five years. Six installments have already been redeemed. This is the seventh installment, with a lottery of ten tickets and a principal redemption of 4 million yuan. (5) The 18th Year of the Republic Disaster Relief Public Bonds had a total issuance of 10 million yuan. Since June of the 18th year of the Republic, they have been redeemed twice annually, with each redemption being one-twentieth of the total amount. Five installments have already been redeemed. This is the sixth installment, with a lottery of five tickets and a principal redemption of 500,000 yuan. (6) The 19th Year of the Republic Customs Duty Public Bonds had a total issuance of 20 million yuan. Since June of the 19th year of the Republic, they have been redeemed twice annually, with each redemption being one-twentieth of the total amount. Three installments have already been redeemed. This is the fourth installment, with a lottery of five tickets and a principal redemption of approximately 1 million yuan. The redemption of all winning bond tickets, except for the Austro-Hungarian Indemnity Secured 24 Treasury Bonds, which are scheduled to begin payment on December 20th, the remaining five types of bond tickets are all scheduled to begin payment on December 31st. The principal and interest due on all winning bond tickets will be paid jointly by the Central, China, and Communications Banks in various locations, along with the interest due on each bond ticket. Please have the supervisors verify the winning tickets and the ticket stubs for execution of the lottery."

Winning Numbers: After the report, the lottery was conducted. The winning numbers for the six types of public bonds are listed below: (1) The 6% Public Bonds of the 7th Year of the Republic: 02, 14, 44, 53, 83. (2) The 24 Treasury Bonds: 09, 14, 39, 63, 71. (3) The Military Needs Public Bonds: 13, 21, 51, 63, 79. (4) The Rehabilitation Public Bonds: 04, 12, 25, 39, 45, 55, 70, 75, 81, 93. (5) The Disaster Relief Public Bonds: 12, 41, 54, 62, 79. (6) The Customs Duty Public Bonds: 16, 28, 47, 56, 87.

Total Redemption Amount: The 7% Public Bonds total 2,250,000 yuan, the Military Needs Public Bonds 515,000 yuan, the Rehabilitation Public Bonds 4 million yuan, the Disaster Relief Public Bonds 500,000 yuan, and the Customs Duty Public Bonds 1 million yuan. The total redemption amount for the six types is 8,385,000 yuan.

Guangdong Fourth Plenary Session Shanghai News

All Delegates Unanimously Approve Mediation Methods

Hu Hanmin Telegraphs That He Will Return to Shanghai After the Election

Xin Sheng She reports that the dispute at the Guangdong Fourth Plenary Session had the potential to be resolved immediately after Hu Hanmin, Wu Chaochu, and others went to Hong Kong to mediate. However, a Hong Kong telegram stated that mediation had completely failed. We now know that the claim of failure is inaccurate. Last night, Hu and Wu telegraphed Shanghai, stating that after submitting three solutions, Deng Ziru, Xiao Focheng, Chen Jitang, and Li Zongren had already agreed to submit the Shanghai Peace Conference proposal, which had been overturned by the meeting on the 24th, to the conference for reconsideration and had taken on the task of communicating with the delegates. At the time, a small number of people still insisted on the original proposal, but after strenuous efforts, there were no more objections. Therefore, on the evening of the 29th, the three individuals who had withdrawn and the delegates returned to Guangzhou. Except for Sun, Hu, and Wu, everyone else returned to the provincial capital. Consequently, a plenary session was held at 8:00 AM yesterday (the 30th), and it was unanimously passed to accept the three mediation methods proposed by Hu, Wu, and others. Sun Ke then returned to Guangzhou yesterday afternoon to attend the meeting after the conference passed the three methods. Hu did not attend and remained in Hong Kong, awaiting the completion of the election before leaving Hong Kong and returning to Shanghai. The text of the telegram released by the Hu residence regarding the acceptance of the three mediation methods by the Plenary Session is as follows: (1) Regarding the election of Chiang Kai-shek as a Central Committee member, it is stated that there are no objections in order to strive for unity. (2) One hundred and twelve Central Committee members of the fourth session are selected from the first, second, and third sessions. (3) The remaining forty-four individuals are freely elected.

The Far East News Agency reports that Hu Hanmin, who went to Guangdong to mediate, telegraphed Wang Jingwei yesterday, reporting on the circumstances of this trip to Guangdong for mediation. The telegram arrived in Shanghai at 4:00 PM yesterday. The original telegram roughly stated that Hanmin and Chaochu arrived in Guangzhou on the morning of the 29th. After paying respects to the late Gu Tingqin, they met with Deng Ziru, Xiao Focheng, Li Delin, Bai Jiansheng, Chen Bonan, and others. As a result, they agreed to accept the peace conference resolution as much as possible and agreed to explain the misunderstandings to the delegates. From the 30th onwards, the conference continued to meet and was scheduled to hold elections on the 1st. Hanmin and Chaochu felt that the mediation had been successful and returned to Hong Kong that evening. They will return to Shanghai with comrades Sun and Wu after the conference closes.

Japanese Residents to Hold a General Meeting

Meeting to Be Held for Three Days Starting Sunday

Representatives from Various Regions Converge in Shanghai

Discussing Ways to Counter Chinese Actions

Since the September 18th Incident, China has been unanimously boycotting Japanese goods. In just a few months, Japanese trade in China has decreased by over 70 million yuan in goods shipped to China. Along the Yangtze River, from Sichuan to Jingzhen, Japanese merchants have withdrawn to Shanghai due to the lack of business. All women and children have been sent back to their country, while many men remain in Shanghai. Therefore, the number of Japanese residents in Shanghai has not only not decreased but has also increased. Since the Tianjin Incident, Japanese ruffians have also considered making trouble in Shanghai, but they have not dared to do so due to our strict defense, which they consider regrettable. Currently, Japanese residents in Shanghai have successively withdrawn from Chongqing, Chengdu, Yichang, Shashi, Changsha, Hankou, Wuhu, Suzhou, Nanjing, Hangzhou, Fujian, and other places, concentrating in one corner, unwilling to give up trade with China. Suddenly, they are advocating for a general meeting of all Japanese people in China to discuss ways to counter Chinese boycotts. How to restore commerce on the Yangtze River? How to support Japanese residents in China? And various other secret proposals. The preparations were first made by Japanese residents in various places in Shanghai. On the morning of the 30th, the inaugural meeting of the All-China Japanese Conference was held at the Japanese Club in Hongkou. Hundreds of representatives attended at the time. It is reported that the conference resolved to send telegrams to various places, urging representatives to come to Shanghai quickly to hold a general meeting. After discussion, it was decided to hold a meeting for three consecutive days, starting on December 6th and closing on the 8th. The reception center for representatives arriving in Shanghai has already been established. Yesterday, according to telegrams from various places, representatives who have already departed for Shanghai include Koyama Teiichi, Chairman of the Fengtian Youth Association Alliance; Mr. Murachi, Chairman of the Qingdao Youth Association; Mr. Sato, representative of Japanese residents in Shandong; and Mr. Shimizu, representative of Changchun. In addition, representatives from Fuzhou, Xiamen, Jiaoji Railway, and others have all telegraphed their departure and are expected to arrive in Shanghai by tomorrow or the day after. It is reported that after the meeting on the 6th, the conference will use the name of the All-China Japanese Residents Conference to submit its proposals to the Japanese Minister to China and will also send representatives back to their country with the resolutions, requesting their government to implement them. According to a certain gentleman familiar with Japanese affairs, this economic severance has dealt a major blow to the Japanese. In just over two months, the Japanese people's years of business in China have been eradicated, causing great losses and pain. Today, there are already signs of military action, and Japanese residents will take further steps to seek permanent benefits. Therefore, this All-China Japanese Conference in Shanghai deserves special attention.

Oppose the Demarcation of a Neutral Zone

Gao Guanwu and Others Offer Opinions

Gao Guanwu and others sent a public telegram, stating, "To all newspapers, agencies, and public organizations, we have investigated the customary practices of war. When the outcome of a battle is uncertain, the intervention of a third country for mediation or arbitration may result in the establishment of a neutral zone. However, the violent Japanese, taking advantage of our natural and man-made disasters, unilaterally attacked and fought without restraint, implementing invasion and seizing our three northeastern provinces. Except for the defensive setbacks of Ma and the brigade, the Liaoning and Jilin armies have not retaliated at all. If we follow the League of Nations and demarcate the area near Jinzhou as a neutral zone, it would be tantamount to admitting that Liaoning and Jilin are lands we have lost due to defeat in war. Such a stipulation is an insult to all the citizens of our country and is absolutely intolerable. Even the barbaric tribes of Africa, once they form a tribe, will resist foreign insults. How can our civilized China be slaughtered at will? The plan for now is to unanimously urge the government to gather strength, unite the top and bottom, and actively prepare: (1) Rectify the police reserve teams and public security teams in all provinces and counties across the country, as well as local militias, to protect the local area and maintain order to prevent bandit disturbances. (2) Deploy the troops from nearby coastal provinces, concentrate their strength, and defend key passes to prepare for resistance. (3) Awaken the public to organize volunteer armies, transportation teams, and rescue teams for use. (4) Recruit retired soldiers to train military officers and talents for dispatch. (5) Recruit local Red Spear Society and Lian Zhuang Hui, intensify training for replenishment. The above points have received little attention from our government, and there is no overall statistic. Divided, their strength is weak; united, their strength is strong. All troops are the armed forces of the people. The top and bottom are of one mind, jointly facing the national crisis. Only then can there be hope of saving the misfortune. These are our foolish considerations, and we humbly contribute our humble opinions. We hope they will be considered and adopted." The telegram was signed by Gao Guanwu, Hong Zhongkai, Qi Wenhua, Xu Baozhang, Chen Weixin, He Menghua, Zheng Shaochen, Chen Zuyi, Shen Yuchun, Ding Bingkun, Xu Huiren, Jiang Xilin, Qiu Peixin, Hu Gongliang, Cheng Shiluo, Yang Chao, Ding Dingyi, Bao Dounan, Yuan Yangshan, Gu Zengwei, Zhang Desen, Wang Keming, Bi Yaohua, Zhou Gangshan, Yang Qingjing, Zhou Jianwu, Jin Luwang, Ren Datong, Zhou Mingqi, Hou Gongran, Wu Fengshan, He Zhong, Sun Qiqing, Nie Xitang, and others.

Establishment of the Anti-Japanese Association's Patrol Teams

Water Patrol Team: Four Squads

Vehicle Patrol Team: One Squad

Water Patrol Team: The Inspection Department of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of this city, after investigating unscrupulous merchants with cold blood, in light of the strictness of inspection work, finds that it is extremely difficult to transport Japanese goods privately by land. In order to avoid attention and escape the law, they do not hesitate to use the dark of night and switch to water transport. Although each precinct and team has been urged to strictly investigate, they suffer from having too few people and are unable to dispatch enough. In particular, it is impossible to investigate and seize goods transported by water at night. In order to step up its work, the department has specially obtained approval from the Standing Committee to organize four water patrol teams, which will provide their own multiple ships and be stationed in places such as Nan Shi's Rihui Port, Zhabei's Lao Port, Shanghai West's Xiaoshadu, and Hongkou. They will specialize in the inspection of Japanese goods on the water. It is reported that Zhang Yaoming has been appointed as the chief captain, and Zhang Huijun, Qian Dongye, Pu Zhiliang, and Cheng Xiwu have been appointed as captains. They will actively prepare from today and are expected to start work within days.

Vehicle Patrol Team: The Inspection Department of the Anti-Japanese Association, recently, in light of the intense work, in addition to ordering each team and precinct to strictly seize Japanese goods day and night, and in order to prevent unscrupulous merchants from transporting Japanese goods privately at night, has specially organized a vehicle patrol team. The chief secretary of the department will concurrently serve as the captain. Each night, he will gather many inspectors, all driving automobiles, and patrol strictly throughout the city all night long. If they encounter Japanese goods, they will seize them in order to prevent anyone from escaping. It is reported that the team has already been organized and will soon implement inspections.

City Chamber of Commerce

Circular Letter Refusing to Load and Transport Japanese Goods

The City Chamber of Commerce yesterday received a letter from the Anti-Japanese Association stating that there are still instances of barges or automobiles loading and transporting Japanese goods in the Huangpu River and on the roads. Yesterday, it specially sent letters to the barge transport, coal and stone barge transport, and automobile transport trade associations, stating that they should all refuse from now on. The two letters are recorded below: (1) Letter to the barge transport and coal and stone barge transport trade associations, saying: On the 30th of this month, we received a letter approved by the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association stating that, according to repeated confidential reports, the source of enemy goods is often unloaded in the Huangpu River and transported by barges to the east and west of the Huangpu River and to various locations along the Suzhou River for landing. We should strictly investigate and prohibit barge owners from loading and transporting such goods. Many parties have come to the Chamber with these concerns. After inspecting the inspection work, we have roughly deployed on land, but there is no prevention on the water, which has resulted in enemy goods still being active. After investigating the cause, we find that if there are no barges to load and transport the goods, how can they circulate? Therefore, the key to the plan is to stop the transportation of goods on behalf of others. After the twenty-third standing committee meeting, it was decided to send a letter to your association to instruct the barge transport trade association to strictly prohibit all barge owners from loading and transporting enemy goods again. If anyone dares to deliberately violate this, they will be severely punished according to the law of joint liability of unscrupulous merchants. The record is on file. Correspondingly, the record is sent to you and you are requested to investigate and forward it accordingly. Approved. We have investigated that the violent Japanese are using military force to occupy our Eastern Provinces, and recently bombed Tianjin, with their violence and coercion reaching their extreme. Anyone with a conscience is filled with anger and determined to avenge this unbearable humiliation. Now, it is said that barge gangs are openly loading and transporting enemy goods in the Huangpu River and secretly selling them in the market. Such people are devoid of conscience and are public enemies in the voices of resisting Japanese goods. It is imperative to strictly prohibit this. In accordance with the previous letter, we are notifying you to investigate and immediately instruct all affiliated businesses that they must not transport these Japanese goods in the future. If anyone still covets petty profits and secretly transports them, they will be punished according to the law once discovered, and this Chamber will not cover for them. Please forward this instruction to everyone for compliance. (2) Letter to the rental automobile trade association, saying: On the 30th of this month, we received a letter approved by the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association stating that, according to repeated confidential reports, various automobile companies in this city often provide vehicles for Japanese businesses and Chinese unscrupulous merchants to transport enemy goods. Please prohibit and severely punish them. Our Chamber's duty officers have also seen this situation frequently. However, due to the speed of the cars, there is no way to intervene. After the twenty-third standing committee meeting, it was decided to send a letter to your association to instruct the automobile transport trade association to strictly prohibit all car companies from transporting enemy goods on behalf of others. If anyone dares to deliberately violate this, they will be punished according to the law of joint liability of unscrupulous merchants. The record is on file. Correspondingly, the record is sent to you and you are requested to investigate and forward it accordingly. Approved. This matter concerns the great plan of resisting Japan and saving the nation. We are sending a copy of the letter to you and urge you to forward it to all automobile companies, instructing them to refuse to load and transport enemy goods in the future. Please do not be blinded by petty profits and cause inconvenience. This is of utmost importance.

Methods for Substituting Japanese Goods' Raw Materials

Divided into Long-Term and Short-Term Categories

The Shanghai National Products Factory Federation yesterday sent a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce saying: In response to your letter pushing for the acceptance of the letter from the Yantai General Chamber of Commerce requesting the association's articles of association and inquiring about the established methods for substituting raw materials, it is mainly divided into long-term and short-term categories. (1) Each factory should provide a detailed list of the quantity and name of Japanese raw materials needed each year. After each industry has gathered the information, it should be ordered from the West on the one hand, and on the other hand, it should find ways to improve and replace the materials with those available in the country. (2) Each should consider the raw materials needed by its own industry. If funds are raised to form a raw material factory, the products produced will be used by the shareholder factories, or the existing raw materials will be invested in cooperation with them to expand and increase production. In accordance with the previous letter, we are enclosing the articles of association with this letter for your reference and forwarding.

It has not yet been decided whether to hold meetings in Shanghai for a long time in the future. Transporting Silver for Export

Customs Has Been Ordered to Prohibit

And Separately Notified the Banking and Money Industries

Local finance has been affected by the export of silver, and the money market has become increasingly tight. Although the Banking and Money Trade Associations have repeatedly convened emergency meetings to discuss prohibition measures, the biggest key to the tight money market is that it is affected by the current situation. Exporting silver is only for the purpose of regulating finance in various places, and there is no situation of being used by the enemy. Therefore, it is difficult to absolutely prohibit it. Now we know that Finance Minister Song Ziwen believes that although the tight money market is said to be related to the insecurity of the current situation, it is also in conflict with the export of silver. Therefore, he issued a general order to customs offices in various places on the previous day (30th) to prohibit the declaration of silver for export. If it is indeed for the purpose of regulating finance, it must also be thoroughly investigated to avoid unscrupulous merchants from cheating, coveting small national profits, and harming the national finance. Otherwise, they will not be allowed to declare for export. The Shanghai Jianghai Customs Superintendent's Office has recently instructed the Tax Affairs Department to comply with it, and has separately notified the Banking and Money Trade Associations for reference and investigation.

This Year's Business Situation of Two Railways

According to recent statistics, the business situation of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus this year is no less than last year. Passenger transport revenue is actually better than last year. However, freight transport has been greatly reduced compared to last year due to the impact of military affairs and floods. As of November of this year, the revenue from passenger and freight transport on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway has reached more than 12 million yuan. It is estimated that another 2 million yuan can be earned by the end of this year. On the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, it can reach more than 9 million yuan.

Freezing of Rivers in Northern China

Discussions to Increase Freight Rates on Tianjin-Bound Ships The weather in North China is gradually getting colder, and the Baihe River in Tianjin is now freezing. Shanghai-bound ships to Tianjin must be guided by icebreakers to enter the port. Therefore, the British merchants Taikoo and Jardine Matheson, and the Chinese merchant China Merchants Steam Navigation Company in this city held a special meeting to discuss the implementation of ice river freight rates from December 1st. After deliberation, the price of foreign cloth and cotton yarn increased from 16.5 taels to 18 taels per ton. The price of wheat flour increased from 1.9 cents to 2.1 cents per bag. The price of groceries increased by 20% per ton across the board. Yesterday, all the guest families were notified.

Yingkou Scheduled to Suspend Navigation There is a large backlog of goods in Yingkou. Shanghai's various shipping companies dispatched a large number of merchant ships to load them last month. Now, a lot of soybeans and sorghum have been loaded and shipped. Yesterday, the shipping bureaus received a telegram from Yingkou, stating that the inner harbor there is frozen. The shipping companies have already agreed that the ship departing from Yingkou on December 6th will be the last batch. The river will be closed from the 7th. Please do not send any more merchant ships to that port. Navigation will resume after the river thaws next year.

Local News Two

Rivaling London and New York's

Shanghai Patrol Cars

Each Car is Equipped with Wireless Telephone

Orders Can Be Received Within Seconds

More Telephones are Set Up in Various Places as Auxiliary Support

Kidnappings by Bandits May Be Reduced

The new wireless telephone patrol cars and one hundred and forty police telephones of the Public Concession Police have been put into use yesterday (30th). From now on, criminals will see that the police's detective patrols are becoming more effective and that it is not easy to escape the law by committing crimes. The Public Works Department spent about 200,000 yuan to prepare this equipment this spring. The police officers have now been trained to maturity. The effectiveness of its use may mean that London and New York will no longer be the only ones to have this capability. There are now a total of twelve patrol cars, with one patrol car assigned to each police district. Each car shed is equipped with an indoor antenna and a wireless telephone receiver and amplifier. In addition, a wireless telephone transmitter and ordinary police telephones are installed on the top floor of the Public Works Department as the management agency. In the event of serious cases such as armed robbery, kidnapping, or theft, after residents within the boundary or various police stations and patrol officers notify the management agency by telephone, a wireless telephone will be issued immediately, and nearby patrol cars will rush to arrest the criminals. Residents can connect to the management agency by telephone in at most five minutes, and patrol cars can receive orders in seconds. After all the police telephones are installed, there will be one hundred and forty units to assist patrol cars and provide alarm and command transmission. Each police station has a central office that manages the police telephones in that district. The management personnel of the police station only need to press an electric key, and each telephone will ring loudly and emit a red light. Nearby patrol police can hear the sound or see the red light and go to answer the telephone.

Shen Chengfu Surrenders Himself

Admitting Business Failure and Debts

Without Any Fraudulent Behavior

Taihe Still Accuses Him of Embezzlement

After the collapse of the Zhihe Yongji Money Shop, the shop's manager Shen Yingxiang and his son Shen Chengfu, the compradore of the British merchant Taihe Foreign Firm, fled without a trace. The creditors generally believed that the Shen family and his son were suspected of colluding to defraud money, and filed lawsuits with the First Special District Court, which issued arrest warrants. Shen Yingxiang was arrested in Shangyu by Geng Debiao, a Chinese detective of the General Patrol Room, and escorted to the Special Court. Shen was ordered to provide a guarantor who could be called at any time and released on bail pending trial. However, Shen Chengfu has not been apprehended to this day. Recently, Shen Chengfu believed that all his debts were due to business failure and that there was no fraudulent behavior, so he returned to Shanghai a few days ago and lived at No. 572 Laoxifu Road in the French Concession. He surrendered himself to the General Patrol Room at 6:00 a.m. yesterday. After investigation by the Patrol Room, it was found that the only party who had filed a complaint against Shen Chengfu with the Patrol Room was Taihe Foreign Firm, accusing him of embezzlement of 3,451,000 yuan. Therefore, Shen was escorted to the First Special Court's Criminal Division One at 9:00 a.m., where Judge Xu Jashi of the Criminal Court presided over the interrogation. Lawyer Ru Baoyi represented Taihe Foreign Firm, and Lawyer Lu Xingyuan represented Wu Linkun Lawyer represented Wanlai Foreign Firm and some of the creditors in the money industry. Shen Chengfu also hired two lawyers to defend him. According to the Patrol Room Lawyer Ru, the Patrol Room is now prosecuting Shen for breach of trust under Article 366 of the Criminal Law. The details can be stated by Ke Pudeng, a representative of Taihe Foreign Firm. However, the detailed accounts of this case have not yet been clarified, so please allow a postponement. Subsequently, Ke Pudeng stated that he is now accusing Shen Chengfu of embezzlement, because his company delivered 20,000 bales of cotton worth 2.7 million taels to Shen, but he embezzled all the money received and paid with a kind of worthless bank note. Judge Xu asked Ke whether he had delivered the goods to Shen and Shen had paid the foreign firm. Ke replied that it was for a term of sixty days. The cotton we gave was a credit loan. Then, Nai Xu testified that Shen had no guarantor in his firm, but he had 130,000 taels in cash and property guarantees. Questioned, Shen Chengfu confessed that the plaintiff said that I embezzled, but it was actually a loss in the cotton business, and I used the money I received to make up for the previous losses, which was completely in accordance with the firm's transfer, and that the departure on August 19 was to collect accounts outside, not to escape. The defendant's lawyer then stated that this case is a matter of accounts and belongs to civil matters. The criminal prosecution of embezzlement cannot be established. Moreover, when the defendant left on August 19, it was still within the sixty-day settlement period, and the plaintiff did not wait until the sixty-day settlement date before accusing Shen of embezzlement to the patrol room. How did the plaintiff know that the defendant wanted to embezzle at that time? Therefore, he requested permission to post bail. Judge Xu Jashi reviewed the confession and ordered that the case be adjourned for a retrial.

A Large Batch of Red Pills Transported to Hangzhou

The Hangzhou Public Security Bureau Cracked the Case

Hong Shaopu Was Arrested Pending Transfer

The Detective Team of the Hangzhou Public Security Bureau learned last month that someone was privately transporting a large batch of red pills from Shanghai to Hangzhou, which were transported by Huitong Transportation Company and delivered to Jiang Shijie, an employee of the Hangzhou Guohua Soap Company. They went to secretly wait. When Jiang Shijie went to pick up the goods at the appointed time, he was detained and four iron barrels of red pills worth more than 10,000 yuan were seized. He was taken to the Public Security Bureau along with the pills. Under questioning, it was learned that the iron barrels were entrusted by the Shanghai Meihua Soap Company to the Shanghai Huitong Transportation Company to be transported to the Hangzhou Huitong Branch for unloading. They went to arrest Chen Zaixin, the manager of the Huitong Branch, and handed him over to the Hangzhou Local Court Procuratorate for investigation. On one hand, the Procuratorate sent a letter to the Hangzhou Public Security Bureau requesting that personnel be sent to Shanghai to arrest Hong Shaopu, the general manager of the Shanghai Huitong Company, a native of Suzhou, and bring him to justice for questioning. On the 27th of last month, Ding Wenbing, the captain of the third team of the Detective Team, took the document to Shanghai, investigated and found it to be true. At 10:30 a.m. on the previous day, he reported to the Huisit patrol room and asked for assistance in arresting Hong Shaopu. The patrol room forwarded the request to the First Special District Court to issue an arrest warrant. Hong was arrested by the Huitong Company at No. 233 Jielu and taken into the patrol room. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Second Criminal Division of the Special Court. According to Patrol Room Lawyer Wang Yaotang, the representative of the Hangzhou Public Security Bureau presented the official document of the Public Security Bureau when reporting to the Patrol Room yesterday. Today, he suddenly presented the official document of the Local Court Procuratorate. Checking the date of the court document, it was November 28, but the defendant Hong Shaopu was arrested yesterday (30th). The date is wrong. This point should be noted. Then, Ding Wenbing, the team leader of the Hangzhou Public Security Bureau, submitted the official document requesting extradition, and said that as for the date, it may have been a misunderstanding, because after arriving in Shanghai on the 27th, I reported to Hangzhou by long-distance telephone that the person had been identified, and Hangzhou had mistaken him for having been arrested. Questioned, the defendant Hong Shaopu hired two lawyers, Ye Fikang and Zhao Weiding, to defend him. Judge Feng Shide ordered Hong to be returned to custody and rescheduled the hearing for two days, pending verification of the official documents.

Reactionary Printed Matter Implicates Widow

Various Businesses Jointly Guarantee Shen Tangshi

Shen Tangshi, a widow from Wuxi, is 42 years old. Her husband died many years ago, leaving behind a nine-year-old daughter. Because of her determination to remain chaste, she opened the Taiheng Confectionery at No. 538 Pushan Road, Zhabei, employing one employee and one apprentice. At 10:00 a.m. on the previous day (27th), an old junk dealer suddenly appeared, peddling old newspapers and books, asking for three yuan per load and eighty cash per catty. Because she was illiterate and greedy for the cheap price, she bought seventy catties for wrapping candies and other items. The neighbors all saw it. At that time, the shop employee Yao Heting went to pick up goods. When he returned to the shop, he saw that the old newspapers and books bought by the landlady were mostly reactionary publications. He told the landlady that they could not be used for wrapping, so as not to cause trouble. He then told the apprentice to throw all the waste books into the nearby river. Unexpectedly, they floated downstream to the Yingpan Bridge, where they were retrieved by a Jiangbei dugout boat. Seeing that the waste paper could be sold for money, they spread it out on the boat shed. Later, a patrol police officer from the Tanjiachiao Police Station in the Fourth District saw it and arrested two dugout boat owners. When asked about the source of the waste books, they did not know either. When asked of the neighbors, they said that they were discarded by Yongtaiheng. Chen, the police officer, was reported and he went to Yongtaiheng and arrested the landlady Shen Tangshi and escorted her to the Fourth District General Office. After a brief interrogation by Director Zhou, because the case was related to reactionary publications, he immediately transferred it to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for handling. However, the nearby stores, such as Yongdagong South Goods Store and more than ten other households, knew that Shen Tangshi was living peacefully and was an ignorant woman who suffered this injustice. Therefore, they jointly elected a representative, Zhou Rong, to report to the Fourth Branch of the Citizens' Association, and affixed their seals in a joint petition to the Public Security Bureau, requesting bail. Party member Zhou Wenbing also reported to Wu Zhen, the executive member of the Second District Party Headquarters, requesting him to prove and rescue her. However, it is heard that the Public Security Bureau has transferred the case to the Garrison Command for review.

Four Organizations

Discuss Anti-Japanese Entertainment Gathering

Expand Propaganda Campaign

Yesterday afternoon around 2 PM, four organizations, including the Chinese Students Returned from Japan Association, the Northeast Natives Association in Shanghai, the Shanghai Private Elementary School Teachers Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, and the Shanghai Drama Troupe Federation, jointly discussed the Anti-Japanese Entertainment Gathering at the Kun Fan Girls' Middle School on Mei Bai Ge Road. Each organization sent five or six representatives, totaling more than twenty people, including Shi Tonggang, Luo Jianbing, Chen Di'ai, Zhao Ming, Ma Zhangnan, and others. Cheng Ming was publicly elected as chairman, and Chen Di'ai as the secretary. The League of Nations is even helping Japanese imperialism to invade our country. Recently, they have been advocating sending international police to China, which is a prelude to imperialism jointly controlling China. If we are not self-aware and even propose a neutral zone in Jinzhou, our compatriots will soon face death. For the sake of saving the country from danger and for our survival, we are initiating this meeting to fully expose the atrocities of Japanese imperialism in China, to inspire the patriotic enthusiasm of the people, and to expand the anti-imperialist movement to divide China. I hope everyone will express their insightful opinions and work together to plan the way forward. As a result, the following resolutions were made: (1) The organizing committee will be divided into three departments: General Affairs, Propaganda, and Entertainment. General Affairs will be the responsibility of the Private Elementary School Teachers Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association and the Northeast Natives Association in Shanghai. (3) The performance venue is planned to be at the Ningbo Natives Association in Shanghai, and the dates are set for December 11th, 12th, and 13th, a total of three days. The General Affairs Department is responsible for contacting them. (4) 5,000 tickets will be printed for the entertainment gathering, with 1,200 tickets given away as complimentary tickets, and the remaining 3,800 tickets will be divided into one-yuan and half-yuan tickets. Half of the ticket revenue will be used to reward the soldiers on the front lines in the Northeast, and the other half will be used to fund the anti-Japanese movement. (5) The content of the dramas will include more than ten programs such as "Liberation," "On the Banks of the Yitong River," "Bloodstained Clothes," and "The Night Before," all of which are excellent dramas to inspire the patriotic enthusiasm of the people. Other programs will be added temporarily. (6) The office location will be located in the Huadong Apartment on Malang Road in the French Concession. Every day from 4 PM to 6 PM will be the gathering time for work. The other items were also discussed in detail. The meeting adjourned around 6 PM.

Using Hundred-Yuan Counterfeit Money

Rice Store Unknowingly Accepts It

All Those Involved Are Detained

Shen Guijin, a worker from Changzhou at the Tianzhang Paper Mill at 408 Yangshupu Road, on the morning of the 26th of last month, along with the factory's gatekeeper Shu Linshun, also from Changzhou, used a Central Bank of China hundred-yuan counterfeit note to buy a担 (dan, a unit of weight) of rice, costing 14.6 yuan, from the Dinghe Rice Store at 343 on the same road, and sent it to the factory. The remaining money was given to Shu Linshun to take away. Unexpectedly, the note was given to a money shop by Dinghe Rice Store the other day, which discovered that it was counterfeit and immediately returned it. Later, it was sent to the Shanghai Bank, but it was also rejected. Unable to redeem it at the Central Bank of China, the teller examined it and found that it was a counterfeit made by using a genuine five-yuan note, and cleverly removing and pasting the red pattern in the middle, making it difficult to distinguish the truth immediately unless one was very careful. Therefore, the rice store reported it to the Huishan Police Station, which sent detective Zhong Deshou to the Tianzhang Paper Mill to arrest Shen and Shu. Xie Bingyao (also from Changzhou), a suspect, was also brought to the police station. According to Shen Guijin's confession, the counterfeit note was given to him by his cohabiting friend Zhang Ruigen to buy rice for him. The detectives then went to 254 Pingliang Road to arrest Zhang, but he had already fled upon hearing the news. The police chief ordered them to be detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. According to Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, the third defendant, Xie Bingyao, was not involved in the use of the counterfeit note, but was suspected of informing Zhang Ruigen to escape, but there was no concrete evidence. The hundred-yuan Central Bank of China counterfeit note was presented for inspection, followed by Song Deji, the representative of Dinghe Rice Store, explaining the situation, and stating that his store and Tianzhang Paper Mill were employer-employee relationships, and that he knew the defendant Shu Linshun and did not suspect that the note was counterfeit. Shen and Shu both testified, stating that they did not know that the note was counterfeit and that all the money had been taken by Zhang. They asked for leniency. Xie Bingyao testified that he knew nothing about the case and did not inform Zhang Ruigen to escape, and retained lawyer Fan Gang for his defense. Judge Shen Bingrong verified the confessions and ordered the three defendants to be remanded in custody pending sentencing.

Shanghai Station Railway Police

Solved a Major Hotel Theft Case in Hangzhou

On November 26th, at the Hangzhou Lakeside Hangzhou Hotel, two guests dressed in luxurious clothes, named Zhan Shusheng and Liu Binglai, checked into Room 22. They stayed for two days and behaved generously, appearing to be officials, so they were not suspected of anything. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 28th, taking advantage of the hotel owner's wife being ill and her husband, Yu Shaofu, going to the hospital, the two men pried open the door lock of the hotel owner's room and used knives to cut open the suitcases in the room, stealing all the cash of more than 300 silver dollars in the suitcases, as well as a large amount of silk clothing, silver tripods, and silver shields. No one noticed. The next morning, the two guests settled their room bills and left the hotel calmly. However, the waiter noticed that the large rattan suitcase and two suitcases they were carrying were unusually heavy, unlike when they first arrived. He then went to their room to investigate and found a copper nail ring left behind. He also checked the hotel owner's room and saw that the door seemed to have been opened. He rushed to the hospital to inform the hotel owner, Yu Shaofu, who returned to the hotel to inspect and found that all the boxes and money were empty. He then realized that he had been stolen from. However, the two guests had disappeared. He immediately reported to the Hangzhou Railway Police Department and the Hangzhou local authorities to request an investigation. The Hangzhou Section Police Department immediately notified the Shanghai South Station Railway Police Department by telephone. Police Chief Zhuang learned of the situation and immediately secretly dispatched Police Sergeant Wang Yubin and a police officer to wait at the Xinlonghua Station for the Hangzhou morning train to arrive and board the train to conduct a secret investigation. They saw two suspicious guests. Because the train was moving, it was inconvenient to take action, so they directly monitored them. When the train arrived at the Shanghai South Station, the two guests were ordering a porter to carry their rattan suitcases and suitcases off the train and out of the station. The police officers immediately stepped forward to stop and interrogate them. The guests initially appeared calm and claimed to be from a government organization. However, when they were asked to open the suitcases for inspection, they found silver shields and women's clothing. After further investigation, their speech became evasive. They were then taken to the police station for strict interrogation, where they confessed to the theft. The police station immediately telegraphed the Hangzhou Section Police Department, which informed the hotel owner, who came to Shanghai by night train upon hearing the news and went to the police station. He identified the seized stolen goods as his lost items. The two suspects were also identified as the hotel guests from the day before. He also stated that there had been many major theft cases in Hangzhou hotels recently, but none of them had been solved. He requested that the suspects be handed over to the Hangzhou local authorities for strict investigation of all cases. The police station then approved the hotel owner Yu Shaofu to return to Hangzhou and obtain an official document from the Hangzhou Police Department and send a police officer to Shanghai yesterday to take the two suspects and the stolen goods to Hangzhou for trial.

Five People Fell into the Huangpu River, Four Rescued

Yesterday morning, in the Huangpu River at the Jiangtian Wharf in Nanshi, a ferry boat was carrying many passengers. Among them was an old accountant, over fifty years old, from Ningbo, who worked at the Dexiang Grain Store at the northern end of Maojia Lane, Doushi Street. He was also carrying a sample bag and was going to Pudong to sample at a foreign firm. Unexpectedly, as the ferry was approaching the shore in Pudong, due to the large number of people and the rapid tide, the boat became unstable. In an instant, a total of five people fell into the Huangpu River. The boatmen and others tried their best to rescue them, and four people were rescued. However, the old accountant from Dexiang Grain Store drowned. Afterwards, the store sent people to try to find the body, but it has not yet been recovered.
