Trial of the Suspects in the Weng Ajiao Case

Weng Ajiao, also known as Wang A, from Ningbo, was hacked to death by enemies leading their followers with axes in the eastern wing room on the upper floor of No. 10 Yuqing Lane, West Xinqiao Street, in the French Concession on the 17th of last month. Now, detectives Jin Jiulin and Zhen Yumin from the Criminal Investigation Unit have learned that the suspects were hiding in a tea shop at No. 651 Chengdu Road in the Public Concession. They went to arrest Zhang Ruiting (also known as Zhang Gezi from Yangzhou), Shuang Fang (from Zhenjiang), Xiao Guifang (from Danyang), and others, and found an axe. They were taken to the police station for further investigation. All the details were reported in detail. In the afternoon, the police sent Zhang and the other two to the First Court of the Second Special Court, where Judge Xiong Hui interrogated them. Gu Shouxi, the police lawyer, explained the case, stating that the defendants still had accomplices who had not been apprehended, and requested that the hearing be adjourned for further investigation. When questioned, Zhang and the other three testified that they were playing mahjong there that night and would not dare to commit murder. Their other words were evasive. They also retained lawyer Zhu Dianqing for their defense. Judge Xiong ordered the adjournment of the hearing and remanded the defendants in custody.

The Premature Lamb Fetus at Nine Acres

Sensational Hearing for a While

It Was Done by Well-Wishers

Around 6 PM last night, two strange fetuses resembling small horses were suddenly discovered at the entrance of the Baosheng Pregnancy Preservation Hospital at No. 125 Luxiangyuan Road, Nine Acres in both cities. This immediately caused a sensation far and wide, and people brought the old and the young to rush to see it. Immediately, the area around Kaiming Lane was crowded with onlookers, and traffic was almost cut off. Some said they had witnessed it being discarded by the hospital, while others said that someone had secretly discarded a premature lamb fetus there to deliberately alarm people. There were many different theories, and no one could agree. Upon hearing the news, the reporter rushed to inquire among the neighbors. Yang Yuhai, the police officer stationed at post No. 1511, who was standing there, said that when the crowd gathered to watch, he pushed through the crowd and saw two bloody fetuses with horse faces and sheep feet, about seven or eight inches long, discarded next to the sewer under the steps of No. 125. When asked, the Baosheng Hospital completely denied it. According to the doctors at the hospital, a woman had been admitted to the hospital three days ago and gave birth to a boy. It has been three days since then, and no one has come to give birth since. Even if there was such a strange birth, the hospital would have preserved it for physiological research and would never have discarded it at the entrance of the hospital, attracting crowds and obstructing traffic. This fact is the most obvious and undeniable. This must be the work of some idle well-wishers who, having nothing to do all day, picked up two premature lamb fetuses from somewhere, secretly threw them at the entrance of the hospital, and deliberately made a sensational scene to attract people to watch, so as to fulfill their secret, self-satisfied, cunning plan. It is extremely boring and not worth a laugh. According to Lin Wenguang, a doctor at the Huiren Clinic across the street from the hospital, one of the discarded fetuses was picked up by an old woman, and the other was wrapped in paper by Chen Zhengling, a Zhenjiang man who buys and sells old goods. However, the truth is difficult to ascertain.

Private Radio Station

Fine of Three Hundred Yuan

The Tianling Company at No. 47 Hehe Lane, Avenue Joffre, in the French Concession, was found by the political department of the French Police to have privately set up a radio station to broadcast and lecture without the permission of the Ministry of Communications. It was deemed to have violated Articles 3 and 4 of the Telecommunications Regulations. The court was requested to issue a search warrant, and detectives were dispatched to search and seize the radio broadcasting station's large and small components. The company's manager, Zhang Jianqiu, was summoned to the First Court of the Second Special Court. The police lawyer filed a lawsuit in accordance with the Telecommunications Regulations, requesting a penalty in accordance with Article 21 of the same regulations. The court ordered the defendant to pay a cash bail of three hundred yuan to be released pending verification. This matter has been reported in previous newspapers. The case has been summoned twice by Judge Wu Fanglian, and the defendant has retained lawyer Yang Guoshu for his defense. The debate has been declared closed, and the verdict is pending. Yesterday was the day of the verdict. The defendant and his lawyer arrived in court at 10 AM to await instructions. Judge Wu presided over the First Criminal Court and summoned the defendant to court for a brief interrogation. Zhang Jianqiu was sentenced to a fine of three hundred yuan for privately setting up a radio station. The seized radio equipment was confiscated as per the list.

Representative to the International Transport Unification Conference

First Open a Transportation Expert Committee

The Chinese Branch of the International Chamber of Commerce Recommends Wu Keyu to Attend

The Chinese Branch of the International Chamber of Commerce previously received a telegram from the Paris headquarters stating that it would convene a transportation expert committee to prepare for the International Transport Unification Conference. The branch consulted and invited Mr. Wu Keyu, a transportation expert, to attend in Paris. Mr. Wu agreed. The relevant telegrams are detailed below: (Telegrams with the Ministry of Communications) To Minister Wang of the Ministry of Communications of the National Government of Nanjing: Approved the International Chamber of Commerce's letter stating that, based on the resolutions of the Washington Conference, the association will unite various international organizations to convene an International Transport Unification Conference within two years. Currently, a transportation expert committee is being organized to be responsible for preparing the Transportation Unification Conference. The development of railway transportation, inland river navigation, highway construction, and aviation, as well as the expansion of electrical applications, are all important topics for the Transportation Unification Conference. You are requested to nominate one expert from the Chinese branch to participate in the aforementioned expert committee and work together. It has been found that your Ministry of Communications has sent a representative to Paris to attend the International League of Nations Transportation Conference. It would be particularly convenient if your branch could obtain the approval of your Ministry of Communications to nominate that expert to serve as your branch's representative. The first meeting of the expert committee is scheduled for mid-November of this year, etc. Based on this, we are inquiring who the representative from your ministry is, whether they are currently in Paris, and whether that expert can be nominated to attend the aforementioned committee. We are sending this telegram to you for instructions. Please provide the expert's name and address, as this is of public interest. Subsequently, a reply telegram was received from the Ministry of Communications stating: Your telegram has been received. Our Ministry has not sent a representative to Paris. The so-called representative may have been sent by the Ministry of Railways. Please inquire directly with the Ministry of Railways. Ministry of Communications. (Telegrams with the Ministry of Railways) To Minister Da of the Ministry of Railways of the National Government of Nanjing: Approved the International Chamber of Commerce's letter stating (omitted). We inquired with the Ministry of Communications in a telegram, and received a reply (see above). Based on this, we are inquiring whether the Chinese representative attending the League of Nations Transportation Conference mentioned by the International Chamber of Commerce was indeed sent by your ministry and whether they are currently in Paris. Can our association nominate that expert to attend the aforementioned committee? We are sending this telegram to you for instructions. If this is indeed the case, please provide the expert's name and address, as this is of public convenience. Subsequently, a reply telegram was received from the Ministry of Railways stating: To the Chinese Branch of the International Chamber of Commerce: Your telegram has been received. Our office director in Europe, Wu Keyu, is currently in Paris. His name and address are K.Y.Woo, 5 Rue Mogador Paris. There is no objection to your association nominating that person to represent your association to attend. As for all matters related to attendance, please consider them accordingly. Best regards, Ministry of Railways. (Telegrams with Mr. Wu) To Mr. Wu Keyu, 5 Rue Mogador, Paris: The Chinese Branch of the International Chamber of Commerce has nominated you to attend the expert committee on transportation unification of the International Chamber of Commerce, which has been approved by the Ministry of Railways. Please accept and reply by telegram. Secretary-General Lin Kanghou. Yesterday, a reply telegram was received from Mr. Wu stating: Your telegram has been received. I will comply and attend. Best regards. (Reply to the International Chamber of Commerce. The association sent a telegram to the International Chamber of Commerce stating: To Mr. Dawson, Secretary-General of the International Chamber of Commerce in Paris: The Chinese Branch has nominated Wu Keyu, the director of the European office of our country's Ministry of Railways, to attend the expert committee on transportation unification. Mr. Wu's address in Paris is 5 Rue Mogador. Please contact him.

Anti-Drug Conference Decides on Important Cases

National Congress Postponed

The China National Anti-Drug Association held a standing committee meeting yesterday, attended by more than ten people, including Wang Jingqi, Cai Rudong, Li Denghui, and Guo Baoyi. Wang Jingqi chaired the meeting. First, the general secretary, Huang Jiaohui, reported on the progress of the association's work. Then, the proposals were discussed, and the following resolutions were made: (1) The National Anti-Drug Representative Congress convened by the association, which was previously resolved to be postponed until January 21, is now being postponed again to March 1, 21, in light of the increasingly tense anti-Japanese issue and the public's anxiety, based on the proposals of anti-drug organizations in various regions. A letter and telegram should be sent to the preparatory offices in various regions at home and abroad, and to all anti-drug associations and anti-drug propaganda associations across the country for reference. (2) Military personnel in Fujian Province are planting opium on a large scale among the Le people in northern and southern Fujian, collecting huge amounts of money, and using airplanes to smuggle and sell opium publicly, harming the people and undermining the ban on opium. Chen Diaoyuan, the chairman of Anhui Province, and Hao Zihua, the director of the Anhui Province Anti-Opium Investigation Department, are also sheltering planting, transportation, sales, and consumption, making the atmosphere of drug use in northern and southern Anhui pervasive, which is heartbreaking. The above incidents have been reported by the heads of anti-drug organizations, people's organizations, and party departments at all levels in Fujian and Anhui, and have been submitted with solid evidence. After investigation by the association, they have been found to be true. Although the association has repeatedly protested and the people of Fujian and Anhui have complained to the National Government, no action has been taken. The association has a responsibility to combat drugs and should continue to protest and request the Central Party Department and the Control Yuan to investigate and deal with the matter according to law, in order to leave the people a glimmer of hope and protect the dignity of the national prohibition law. It was resolved that the secretariat should actively handle the matter. (3) The association's work plan for the eighth to tenth fiscal years was reviewed and approved and will be submitted to the National Congress for discussion in the future. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

The Minzhi Bookstore

Layoff of a Large Number of Workers Case

The Municipal Government Sets the 5th for Arbitration

Regarding the case of the Minzhi Bookstore headquarters laying off all 24 workers in the typesetting department, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has repeatedly convened conciliation committees to conduct conciliation with the Municipal Party Department and the Public Security Bureau. The employer's reason is that the workers in the typesetting department were hired by the foreman. During the strike, the workers posted slogans and overthrew the foreman, causing the foreman to resign in anger, and they insisted on not allowing them to return to work. The workers' reason is that the wages of the workers in the typesetting department were all paid by the factory, not hired by the foreman, and they should not be dismissed illegally on that pretext. However, due to the insistence of both parties, the matter could not be resolved and conciliation was declared unsuccessful. It was submitted to arbitration. The Labor Arbitration Committee of the Municipal Government has approved the submission to arbitration and has scheduled an arbitration meeting for 2 PM on the afternoon of the 5th.

The Dadong Bookstore

Refuses to Negotiate on Its Own

The Company Sets a Deadline for Calculating and Taking Back Wages

After the strike of all employees of the Dadong Bookstore headquarters in the city, it has been sixteen days and they have not yet returned to work. In order to comply with the orders of the party and government organs, the company announced the dismissal of employees who have not returned to work, setting a deadline for them to calculate and take back their wages. However, all employees have vowed not to return to work until the treatment conditions are resolved, and have issued a statement in the newspaper denying the company's illegal announcement. Various labor unions have rallied to their aid and are willing to support them. The Dadong branch office sent representatives Yang Mingqiu, Sun Fenglin, Zhou Minde, Xu Xinong, and others to the company to negotiate with manager Shen Junxin, but they were refused. All the employees were very angry upon hearing this and will make further expressions. It is said that the company has had to suspend operations due to the workers' strike and has suffered considerable losses to date.

Central Bank Inspection Report

One Hundred and Ninth Time

The Central Bank's 109th issuance reserve inspection report states: This council is responsible for inspecting the issuance and exchange coupon reserve of this bank in accordance with the provisions of Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations. The 109th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on November 30, 1931, and the inspection results are announced as follows: (A) Total issuance of exchange coupons: 33,616,924 silver dollars, including 30,947,712 silver dollar coupons and 2,669,212 transfer coupons. Total exchange coupon reserve: 33,616,924 silver dollars, including 23,124,404 silver dollars in cash reserve. The cash reserve is kept in the bank's issuance vault at 17,398,958 yuan, in branch banks at 2,088,228 yuan, and in other banks at 3,637,218 yuan. Guarantee reserve: 10,492,520 silver dollars. (B) Total issuance of customs gold exchange coupons: 500,000 yuan. Total customs gold exchange coupon reserve: 500,000 yuan. The reserve includes 200,000 US dollars, which is kept in local banks and is converted to customs gold at a fixed price of 40. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank's exchange coupon regulations, the cash reserve is 60 percent and the guarantee reserve is 40 percent. The inspection results show that the cash exceeds 60 percent and the guarantee is less than 40 percent, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is made. November 30, 1931, Chairman of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank Li Fuxun, Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilong.

Zhang San Dies from Severe Injuries

Zhang San, also known as Gong Wu, a native of Guangdong, was 30 years old and worked as a peddler. At 6:45 AM on the 18th of last month, he had a quarrel and fight with a fellow villager, a boy named Wan Guifeng, also known as Fan Guifeng (16 years old this year, studying the art of magic), over gambling on the third floor of building number 50 on Xixinqiao Street in the French Concession. Wan stabbed Zhang in the right chest with a sharp knife. Patrolman number 205 arrested Wan, seized the murder weapon, and took him to the police station. Zhang was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment. The police sent Wan to the Second Special Court for prosecution under Article 293 of the Criminal Code for assault. He was ordered to be detained pending further questioning after the victim recovered from his injuries. Zhang died from his injuries at 3:00 PM the day before yesterday. The hospital notified the police, who sent detectives to transport the body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch hall for an autopsy. As there were no relatives of the deceased, the Second Special Court was notified yesterday morning. Prosecutor Ding Shikui, accompanied by a forensic scribe, arrived at the scene and determined that the deceased had indeed died from a knife wound inflicted during his lifetime. The police sent the defendant to court. Mr. Ding interrogated Wan, who confessed that he stabbed the deceased in self-defense because the two men were hitting him. The official ordered the body to be handed over to Tongren Fuyuan Hall for burial, and the defendant was taken back to the police station to await interrogation. After the autopsy, the police photographed the body and had the hall bury it pending identification by relatives.

Shen Shiyong, a calligrapher and painter, is a talented artist with a renowned reputation. New Tiger-Shaped Crab Arrives at the Great World

The owner of the Great World Amusement Park recently obtained a tiger-shaped crab from Tibet. Its color is crystal clear and slightly yellow. The eyes on its back are bright and piercing, resembling a tiger's head. It is very different from ordinary crabs with eyes arranged in a pattern. According to sources in Tibet, this crab is a rare item. The locals call it the "auspicious crab." The locals who see it consider it auspicious. It was once kept at a living Buddha's residence. Recently, people in Shanghai have been flocking to admire it.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday said that the Shandong coast and the Yangtze River basin would be cloudy and foggy, or even rainy. The area south of Ma'an Island would be sunny. There would be strong northeasterly winds over the Yellow Sea and the East China Sea. There is a low-pressure system in Jiangxi. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 64.4 degrees and the lowest was 41.2 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 43.5 degrees and the lowest was 36.0 degrees.

Since October 22nd, this column has raised four questions to solicit opinions, namely (1) regarding the League of Nations, (2) regarding the boycott of Japanese goods, (3) regarding the volunteer army, and (4) regarding uniting the people to face foreign aggression. In the past month, we have received many replies. Those that have been published in this column, such as Mr. Lin Yifang, Mr. Liu Boyong, Mr. Zhongxia, and Mr. Zheng Hongsheng on the boycott of Japanese goods, Mr. Qingyuan on the volunteer army, and Mr. Ding Jichan on uniting to face foreign aggression, all have great value. In addition, there are still many that could not be published due to space limitations. Now that the situation has changed drastically, the national crisis is becoming more urgent. Negotiations with the League of Nations have completely failed. The bitter battle in Heilongjiang Province has finally fallen. Disturbances in Tianjin continue unabated. In this moment when the fate of China is hanging by a thread, simply worrying, being anxious, and being irritable are all useless. All of our citizens should stand up, muster deep courage, and rack their brains to come up with a more appropriate plan for the current major issues and contribute it to the authorities and the people. Now, please raise two questions as follows: (1) Japan's trampling on Heilongjiang Province and its invasion of the Middle East route is not only disregarding our country's sovereignty but also provoking Soviet Russia. According to common sense, Soviet Russia can no longer tolerate it. If it joins the war, the Russo-Japanese War of twenty-seven years ago will be re-enacted. At that time, what attitude should our country take towards Japan and Soviet Russia? If it involves European and American countries, how should we deal with each country? (2) National Government Chairman Chiang has decided to set off for the north to recover lost territory in the coming days. This is certainly what the people of the whole country are eagerly looking forward to. From then on, the overall situation will change drastically. Of course, the government is responsible for military preparations. On the part of the people, what responsibilities and work should they do? What should be done to boycott Japanese goods and train the volunteer army? Each answer should be limited to a maximum of one thousand words, speak less empty words, and focus on proposing methods. This newspaper will disclose the best ones according to the capacity of this column and open them for discussion. If you agree with the methods proposed by others, please also state it. Please also state your name, gender, age, occupation, or school, hometown, attach a communication stamp, and a corresponding number of stamps so that those who are not published in the newspaper will be informed. As for the three questions of schooling, occupation, and marriage, they will still be handled in accordance with the previous regulations. Respectfully.

Letter

Dear Sir, I respectfully write to you to inform you that I and my classmates went to Beijing to petition on the 25th. We had many feelings in all aspects. Although we suffered a lot, we felt that we did not fail this trip. Now there is one thing that is most heartbreaking, briefly described below. After I petitioned the National Government, a Nanjing classmate suddenly mentioned a person from Heilongjiang who was asking for help. He claimed to be a subordinate of Ma Zhanshan and described how he had been inspected several times by violent Japan before he was able to escape from the encirclement and come to Beijing from Ping to ask for help. As for the current situation in Heilongjiang, it is extremely panic. Ma Zhanshan's department can be delayed for up to a month. If the central government does not find a way to remedy it, I am afraid that Heilongjiang will not be able to hold on for long. As for the Heilongjiang army, there are still thousands of people, but there are insufficient military supplies and poor military equipment. Moreover, with the Japanese army pressing on the border, they cannot resist for long. As for the equipment of the Japanese army, it is even more complete. In one division, there are machine gun teams, heavy artillery teams, armored car teams, tank teams, airplane teams, gas teams, etc. When they attack the Heilongjiang army most fiercely, they use poison gas bombs to defend against the enemy, or airplanes drop poison gas bombs, so the dead and wounded are everywhere and in a mess. Even more painful is that the wounded soldiers are captured by the Japanese and shot immediately. Fortunately, they are rescued by the soldiers in the rear. However, the doctors are inadequate, the medicine is bad, and the nurses are also out of shape and scolding them. This is especially unbearable for the soldiers on the front line. Therefore, good men willingly give up, and they feel deeply disappointed and discouraged about the future of the country. Hearing this, I could not help but burst into tears. The brave soldiers of Heilongjiang, who are donating their lives for the country, are being treated so badly by the rear doctors. How can patriotic youths not find a way to help and rescue them? Therefore, please publish it in the newspaper for the examination of colleagues in the medical field. Wang Yuan respectfully writes, "Attached, if there are any medical colleagues who do not avoid hardships and are determined to go to help with medicine, I propose to withdraw money from the donations to Ma Zhanshan to purchase medicine and pay fees." Respected Sir, I read the Benbu News in your newspaper on November 29th about the Pingmin Bank, which mentioned that Liu Zhi initiated it. I have just been informed by Liu, the chairman of our provincial government, that I have no commercial experience and have not heard about the organization of the bank. This news must be a rumor. I urge your newspaper to correct it. I hereby inform you and ask the editor to correct it, Secretary Xu Wenjing of the Henan Provincial Government, December 1st, 20th year.

Dear Editor, I hereby write to inform you that I have read in the Benbu News of your newspaper on the 29th of this month the news that Dafeng Rice Store defrauded money. Our store is also located on Zhoujiazui Road, also named Dafeng, and is also a double-opening store. However, our store is located at 859-60, the east end of Zhoushan Road. The store is located at the Oujia Road intersection. After the incident occurred, many relatives and friends came to inquire after seeing the newspaper. I am sincerely afraid of confusing the rumors and affecting the reputation of the store. Therefore, I am writing this letter to request that it be published in the Letter Column to clarify it. I am very grateful for your kindness. The Dafeng store writes, December 1st.

Respectfully, I am now reading today's newspaper about the exposure of the behind-the-scenes of the Gambling Party. After investigation, our hotel has never had such a thing happen, and Jiang Zhichao and Hua Chunshan have never stayed in our hotel. I am sincerely afraid of confusing the facts, and I should prepare a letter and ask the newspaper to publish it in the Letter Column for correction. I hereby send my best regards to the Editor-in-Chief of Shenbao. Sincerely, Zhongnan Hotel, December 1st.

Automobile News

Special Articles

Achievements in Road Construction in Fujian Province · Learn · Move

Since Xu Xianshi took office as the Director of Construction in Fujian Province in the 17th year of the Republic of China, he planned to build five main trunk roads in Fujian Province. He also raised 40 million yuan in highway bonds as construction costs. This bond was to be raised over five years, with 8 million yuan raised each year. The plan was approved by the provincial government. However, in recent years, Fujian Province has experienced successive political upheavals, banditry, and natural disasters. The fundraising for highway bonds has been delayed and has not been implemented. Several months ago, Yang Shuzhuang proposed to start raising the first phase of highway bonds of 8 million yuan. Although it was approved by the provincial government, disasters have occurred frequently in the past two months. This initiative has been shelved again. However, although highway bonds could not be raised due to various reasons, the Construction Department established highway engineering offices in various sections, assigned laborers to each section, and used the income from highway surcharges to subsidize the expenses of each engineering office. Therefore, the trunk roads that have been completed previously have reached 1,085 li. Those nearing completion reach 475 li. Those yet to be constructed are 2,460 li. (The five trunk lines total 4,020 li). The details are as follows:

(1) Fujian-Zhejiang First Trunk Line. This line runs from Minhou, passing through Lianjiang, Luoyuan, Ningde, Xiapu, and Fuding counties, and enters Zhejiang. The entire line is 100 li long. Currently, only the Minhou-Lianjiang section, which is 40 li, has started construction. This section will be completed soon. (2) Fujian-Zhejiang Second Trunk Line. This line runs from Nanping, passing through Jian'ou, Pucheng, and enters Zhejiang. The entire line is 540 li long. Currently, 60 li between Nanping and Jian'ou has been completed. Also, 5 li between Pucheng and Xianyang Town has been completed. The remaining sections will be under construction. (3) Fujian-Guangdong Trunk Line. This line runs from Minhou, passing through Fuqing, Putian, Jinjiang, Tong'an, Longxi, Zhangpu, Yunxiao, and Zhao'an, and enters Guangdong. The entire line is 1,128 li long. The sections that have been completed and opened to traffic are: Minhou to Changsi Ridge, which is 40 li; Changsi Ridge to Jiangkou, which is 80 li; Jiangkou to Fengting, which is 126 li; Fengting to Luoyang, which is 92 li; Luoyang to Tong'an, which is 155 li; Tong'an to Jiaowei, which is 92 li; Jiaowei to Zhangzhou, which is 68 li. The remaining 62 li will be completed within the year. The Zhangpu to Yunxiao section has been completed for 58 li. The remaining 70 li has also begun construction. In addition, there is the Yunxiao to Zhao'an section, which is 136 li, which has not yet started construction. The Construction Department has sent personnel to prepare for it. (4) Fujian-Jiangxi First Trunk Line. This line runs from Minhou, passing through Nanping, Shunchang, Shaowu, and Guangze, and enters Jiangxi. The entire line is 982 li long. Among them, the completed sections are: Minhou to Muyuan, which is 15 li; Jiulitan to Nanping, which is 35 li; Shaowu to Guangze, which is 20 li. The remaining 35 li will be open to traffic within the year. (5) Fujian-Jiangxi Second Trunk Line. This line runs from Longxi, passing through Nanjing, Longyan, Changting, and enters Jiangxi. The entire line is 660 li long. Currently, the completed section is Zhangzhou to Shuichao, which is 80 li. The remaining 60 li will be open to traffic within the year. The Shuichao to Longyan section is 70 li, and the remaining 68 li has been surveyed and will be under construction. The Tingzhou to Gucheng section is 16 li, and the remaining 40 li is under construction. Among the above lines, the Fujian-Guangdong Trunk Line is almost completed. However, places such as Luoyang Bridge and Wuli Bridge still need to be rebuilt with new-style bridges, which will cost a considerable amount. The Provincial Highway Bureau is planning this. It is expected that the opening of the entire line will not be far away. In addition, the branch lines recently completed by Longxi, Hui'an, Siming, Dongshan, Changtai, Longyan, Zhangpu, Nanjing and other counties are about 500 li. The branch roads in other counties that are being surveyed and constructed are no less than 400 or 500 li. In this time of frequent disasters and urgent foreign troubles, when everything is at a standstill, it is commendable that the road construction in Fujian Province has achieved such results. As for the various highways in the province that were completed two years ago, such as Jinglin Road, Zhangjiu Road, Zhangjing Road, Zhangnan Road, Zhangban Road, Zhangzhuang Road, Zhangjing Road, Zhangwu Road, Taipu Road, Quanyuan Road, Quanyong Road, Shanping Road, Jiangjiao Road, Taiyan Road, Guan Hong Road, Jing Shan Road, etc., which amount to about 600 or 700 li, are not included. Therefore, as of today, the total number of trunk roads, branch roads, and county roads that have been opened to traffic in Fujian Province has reached more than 2,000 li.

1932 Style

A Glimpse of New Cars of Various Brands · Yu

Another year has passed easily. It is the end of the year again. Time flies, no different from the driving of a car. It goes by in a blink of an eye and is fleeting. Therefore, automakers in Europe and the United States have already arranged their new car plans at the beginning of the year. Drivers only need to purchase and choose as they wish. The following is a summary of the new cars of various companies in 1932, as an aid to those who want to buy a car.

Morris Cars: The famous British-made Morris brand new car has already been shipped to Shanghai. It will soon be available for viewing in the showroom. The reputation of Morris cars has always been quite well-known. There is no doubt that the new car is a carefully crafted product of the Morris factory. Regarding the style and appearance, it is naturally superior. As for the improvements and progress, it is difficult to describe them all. Morris cars are manufactured in Cowley, Oxford, England. The cars they make are divided into four main categories: Morris Minor, Morris Major, Morris Cowley, and Morris Oxford. Each category is further divided into six models, so there are many styles in total. According to the dealers selling this brand, the number of new cars coming to Shanghai will not be very large, and there is a risk that demand will exceed supply. As for the reason, it is said that the first is that when new cars are launched, the types that are shipped initially are not very many, but the number of people who need new cars is bound to be large, resulting in insufficient distribution. Moreover, the new models of cars made in the United States often have to wait until the New York Auto Show held in January is over before the new cars are released for sale. During this period, buyers are naturally more eager to buy. The second is that the price of silver has risen, and the selling price has been reduced, so buyers will be even more enthusiastic. Moreover, Morris has long been famous, so there will be many buyers. As for the factory's products, they are first sold domestically and then shipped overseas, so there will not be a large amount of exports for a while. There are many new car styles, such as two-seater sports cars and four-door sedans, which are particularly noteworthy. Regarding the style, the radiator of the 1932 Morris car is made of chrome, which is bright and pleasing to the eye, and the form is beautiful. All six-cylinder models have chrome-plated automatic window panels. Safety is also a major consideration for the new car. The windshield and windows are equipped with a three-piece safety glass device. The fuel tank is installed at the rear and lower part of the frame and does not come into contact with the passenger compartment. The front of the new Morris sedan is "windproof," which not only enhances the appearance but also isolates wind and maintains engine power.

Standard Cars: Standard cars are also among the best British-made cars. The factory has 28 years of car manufacturing experience, so its products are outstanding and highly praised by buyers. The 1932 new car has already started its journey to Shanghai and will arrive soon. The new car has many improvements in the mechanical aspect, which is very suitable for the modern economic trend. As for its comfort, beauty, and low price, they are all the more so. The 1932 Standard cars include four types: Standard "Twenty," Standard "Sixteen," Standard "Big Nine," and Standard "Small Nine." The characteristics of this type of car, which were previously unique to large and expensive cars, are all incorporated into the Standard brand. For example, in terms of the fuel tank, it is installed under the frame for absolute safety. Shock absorbers are installed at the front and rear of the car body. In addition, the wheel lines, windshields, etc. have all been innovated. As for fuel economy and low price, they are unmatched by other cars with the same comfort. This car is very convenient to drive and manage, so women especially like to use it. The brakes are also very powerful. When used, a single touch has a miraculous effect. The car body of the new Standard car is particularly well-made, with spacious seats, convenient access, and ample lighting. The car has four doors, which are beautiful and comfortable. The paint on the car body is particularly eye-catching. The radiator of the new car is very beautiful in style, and the most convenient thing is the roof device. This type of roof is called the Stanlaite type. It can be easily opened and closed by simply turning a knob. It can also be operated safely even when the car is moving.

Graham: According to news from Dodge, the 1932 Graham new car is a six-cylinder model, and its selling price is very low. The new car has many advantages, which cannot be fully described for a while. Let's just mention the most important ones. This car is a six-cylinder model, and it is stable and fast when moving, with no vibration. The car is also equipped with a free wheel, the wheelbase is increased, and the car body is large, so the driver has a comfortable feeling everywhere. As for the beauty of the car body style and the reform of the engine, users will be satisfied.

Willys Cars: The new Willys six-cylinder bus and the C-157 commercial car, with a 157-inch wheelbase, are new products of Willys-Overland. In addition, there is the C-131 with a load capacity of 1.5 tons and the C-113 with a load capacity of 0.5 tons. The body styles of all these new cars are suitable for industrial and commercial use, and they are very economical to use. The new car is a six-cylinder model with the latest 65-horsepower engine. The hydraulic device is particularly characteristic. The half-ton and 1.5-ton trucks are equipped with four-speed transmissions and internal expansion four-wheel brakes. The new car is very durable in use.

Hudson Cars: Hudson Essex cars are very popular. Since Mr. Spalding was appointed as the engine planner, the 1932 new car has many characteristics. Mr. Spalding has many years of experience in planning and manufacturing cars. He is not only famous in the United States, but also admired in Europe. Therefore, the 1932 Hudson new car, once Mr. Spalding pointed it out, was焕然动人(idiom: completely transformed), with beautiful style and smooth movement. In recent years, Mr. Spalding has planned the manufacture of cars for celebrities all over the world. The most famous ones are King Alfonso of Spain, New York Mayor Jimmy Walker, Elizabeth Arden, Roger Wolfe Kahn, Mary Pickford, Lock Sher, Tom Mix, Bainard Walter Flight, Pauline Frederick, Conrad Nagel, Douglas Fairbanks, Charlie Chaplin, and Shalewa Neal.

Studebaker: The Studebaker car produced by Chrysler is very popular and widely used in the market. According to the latest news, 55 new Studebaker cars will be sold in Shanghai. The second batch will arrive in Shanghai soon. The new car has many characteristics and is equipped with free wheels. It is expected that because of the strong demand, it will be very popular once it arrives in Shanghai. In addition, the 1932 new car of the DeSoto six-cylinder model has also begun to be displayed. The DeSoto new car is also equipped with free wheels. The eight-cylinder DeSoto will also meet the people of Shanghai soon. The Packard car is a car with a very good reputation. The 1932 model is even more refined, which is impressive. The sample car has been displayed. Once you inspect it, you will know that the three elements of gorgeousness, comfort, and safety are not empty words. The biggest feature of the Packard new car is its light and flexible driving and management. No matter what the road conditions, the number of passengers in the car, or the climate changes, the Packard car can always provide unexpected comfort and stability. Because its shock absorption device is superior in every way. The Chrysler 1932 new car model has also arrived in Shanghai. However, only the six-cylinder model is available, and the eight-cylinder model has not yet been shipped.

Dodge New Cars: Dodge cars are planned and manufactured by the Dodge brothers. They are very popular and have a very good reputation. The 1932 new car has also been launched. It is said to be the best of Dodge's car manufacturing achievements over the years. Among them, the eight-cylinder new car is the best, with 76 horsepower, so the power is huge and the movement is smooth. The engine is an L-head type, and the cylinders are arranged in parallel. The fuel is very economical when used. As for the beautiful appearance, it goes without saying.

Detailed Record of the International Auto Show · Shadow · Dai

The British Summer Olympia Auto Show, which was once widely publicized, officially opened on November 5th. At this time in the UK, there is a great economic panic, and various industries have shown signs of decline. However, the automobile industry, as evidenced by this international auto show, has obviously made great progress. I will record the various grand occasions to enrich this publication. I think it will also be welcomed by those who are concerned about the automobile industry.

Manifestation of Success: In the past year, various businesses in the UK have declined day by day. However, the UK's automobile industry is the opposite of other industries. It has actually made great success. This is really beyond our expectations. Today, the UK's automobile industry has ranked fourth among the various large enterprises in the country. Moreover, from the recent domestic sales and the proof of overseas trade, it is clear that there is still a major development in the future. Today's transportation industry is developing day by day, and the need for cars is naturally expected. Recently, the number of British cars exported has greatly increased compared with previous years. Therefore, in the past two years, the automobile industry has obviously been able to guarantee future development. Even in the most recent six months, the number of cars imported by Australia, New Zealand, and South Africa that were manufactured in the UK has accounted for 29%. However, if we look back at the situation two years ago, the number of British cars imported in the above-mentioned areas was less than 12%.

Efforts in Economy: The International Auto Show held in London this time has given us great satisfaction. Otherwise, regardless of whether it is inside or outside the UK, the people who visit will be deeply impressed. Moreover, the fact proves that the products of British car factories in this auto show, regardless of any type, have shown success. The main problem is to adapt to the social environment. In other words, it is to be in line with economic principles. At the Summer Olympia Auto Show, we have deeply understood that all cars from various factories can meet economic principles. Moreover, there are countless improvements in various new cars. The car 奥 is wider than the car width, and the selling price is lower than that of the old car. It has done its best to be cheap and beautiful. It is really something that products from various countries cannot match.

Attention to Safety: In recent cities, the number of vehicles coming and going has been increasing day by day. The speed of cars has also been evolving day by day due to the progress of engine manufacturing. Therefore, whether driving is safe has become the main problem. Even the smallest vehicles are exceptionally fast when driving. (To be continued)

News

General Situation of the Xiang-E-Xi Line Project · Mountain · Wave

The Xiang-E-Xi Line is one of the seven major trunk lines in Hunan Province. It runs from Changsha, passing through Ningxiang, Yiyang, Changde, Lixian, and Jinshi, to reach Public Security and Shashi in Hubei. It connects Xiangsha into a provincial road and can directly reach Shaanxi. The total length is 595 li. The Changning section of 100 li has been completed, and the Ningchang section of 308 li is under construction. The estimated cost of the entire road is: roadbed 555,500 yuan, bridges and culverts 595,000 yuan, pavement 476,000 yuan, land purchase, relocation, demolition compensation, etc. 238,000 yuan, surveying 29,750 yuan, engineering office expenses 178,500 yuan, station, shed, telephone pole line fees 89,250 yuan, totaling about 3,142,000 yuan. If no special circumstances are found, this number should not be far off. The project is carried out in three phases. The first phase starts from October of the 18th year to

Ford Cars in Annam

The picture shows a part of the Ford vehicles owned by a car company in Annam. The owner of the company is very satisfied with the operation.

Page 17

June of the 19th year. The roadbed of 320 li from Ningxiang to Changde and the construction of bridges, culverts, and paving with sand, etc., will be completed. The second phase will start from July of the 19th year to June of the 20th year. The roadbed of 205 li from Changde to Jinshi and the bridge and culvert project will be completed. The third phase will start from July of the 20th year to June of the 21st year. The paving with sand of 205 li from Changde to Jinshi and the station, shed, telephone, and other projects will be completed. And continue to complete the various projects of 70 li from Jinshi to the Hubei border. By this time, the entire road will be completed. However, whether it can be completed on schedule depends on whether the project progresses without obstacles. The first section of the Xiang-E-Xi Line is the Changning section. In February of the 15th year, the Xiangzhong Road Bureau first proposed to build it. But it only lasted for ten months before it was suspended due to some reason. In July of the 17th year, the construction was continued. In August of the 18th year, the road line from Yingwan City on the opposite bank of Changsha City, passing through Wangchengpo, Qiaotoupu, Shanzaopu, Bairuopu, Huangnipu, Youcaopu, Xialuopu, and Lijingpu to Ningxiang City, was completed. The total length is 100 li. After being taken over by the Hunan Provincial Highway Bureau, it was renamed the Changning section of the Xiang-E-Xi Line. From Changsha to Zheruopu, which is 50 li, due to avoiding floods, entering and exiting the mountains, detours, and twists and turns, the project is quite large. From Bairuopu to Ningxiang, which is 50 li, passing through the fields, the route is straight and flat, and the project is relatively less expensive. The total span of the bridges in the entire section is 730 feet. Wanglu Bridge is composed of a middle hole with a span of 40 feet, two side holes with a span of 30 feet each, and small urns with a span of 8 feet. The bridge deck is 40 feet higher than the riverbed. The entire structure is made of reinforced concrete, which is simple and strong. It is a new-style building in Xiangzhong, and it leans against Yuelu in the back and overlooks the Xiang River in the front. The clouds, mountains, and green water are beautiful. Sanlilun Bridge has three urns with a span of 8 feet. Qiaotoupu Bridge has four urns with a span of 8 feet. Bairuopu Bridge has one urn with a span of 20 feet. Jingma Bridge has three urns with a span of 30 feet. Since there is no suitable stone material nearby, sandstone and shale are used. During the flood season in Longzhong, the Wei River rises frequently and is often submerged. There are many unique bridges. In addition to Chonggong Bridge with three urns with a span of 20 feet and Shahe Bridge with five holes of a track girder flat bridge with a span of 20 feet, 20 small urns are built to discharge the rapids. The stone material is Carboniferous limestone green stone. Wherever there are streams, small bridges are built, divided into two types: square holes with spans of 2 feet and 4 feet, and arched urns with spans of 4 feet, 6 feet, and 8 feet. The size is determined according to the flow of each river port. The materials are mainly steel bars, cement, and square stones, supplemented by lime, green bricks, and red sand. Earthenware pipes are installed in the farmland waterways to facilitate irrigation. The paving materials are divided into crushed stone and pebbles. The former is more. Wangchengpo to Huangnipu, which is 50 li, is shale crushed stone. The material is fragile and needs to be repaired from time to time, which is a disadvantage. The maximum slope of the road surface is 4%. Along the sides of the road, tung trees and willows are planted for shade. Seven sheds and telephone poles and lines have been built. However, the station is a temporary building. The total cost of the entire section is 310,000 yuan. The average is about 3,100 yuan per li. It is classified as: surveying salary of 10,000 yuan, earth and stone 70,000 yuan, culvert pipes 18,000 yuan, bridge urns 50,000 yuan, Wanglu Bridge 22,000 yuan, paving with sand 80,000 yuan, construction salary 58,000 yuan. In addition, the cost of the station and shed is 5,000 yuan. In addition to the materials, the remaining administrative expenses could have been reduced somewhat. However, due to changes in the plan midway, it was delayed for four years before it was completed. Therefore, the cost was slightly higher. This section starts in the provincial capital and ends in Ningxiang. One is the political and economic center, and the other is the main road for water and land transportation. Therefore, after the completion of the highway, it is more convenient for travelers along the way, and the commercial activities are more prosperous. (To be continued)

The Art World

Recent Italian Literary Scene

— Mo Jing

Six Italian Novels

The first book we want to introduce is "Il Sob A Picco" by Di Vincenzo Cardarelli, a memoir-like novel. Cardarelli's writing is so charming and simple that readers are reluctant to put it down. The book begins like this: "The village where I was born, where I spent my childhood, a part of my youth, the village where I first knew love, was once called Corneto, Tarquinia. If I close my eyes, my first memory is of that old house, surrounded by a garden, and in the corner of that garden is...a magnolia." Personal recollections are often the most beautiful subjects in literature, especially in Italian literature. The book begins in this way, and the reader can be sure that it is worth reading. Because when an Italian writer reminisces about his hometown or the house of his childhood, he often writes his best work.

This book mostly describes Corneto, which is located on a mountain in the Maremma region. In this book, we can see the picturesque, bare, gray, and misty scenery around the village, the pleasant slopes, the interspersed gardens and trees, and the lively San Antonio festival in the village, with mule races. We can also hear the desolate monotony of its only song. We are even more like eyewitnesses to the many intruders who come to Corneto every year: the harvesters in blue, the diggers and cleaners of Agilent, the harvesters who come in mid-July, then the charcoal burners, and finally the shepherds. There are two very beautiful portraits: one of Argentone, the manager of a group of wandering workers, a short, conceited man; and the other of Redagna, the declining landowner, a faithful companion to the whole region, and a storyteller. In such a place, and in the stories of his father's snack shop at the station, or in the portrait of the old stonemason of Solitudessetiognano, Cardarelli gives us that true, permanent Italy, which most foreigners never see, or, even if they see it, they forget. This book was awarded the Premio Bagutta in 1930.

The second book is "Il Paradiso Perduto" by Alberto Cacocci. Cacocci writes best when he writes simply and without extravagance. For example, how well he describes a June evening in his childhood, when dinner was over and his family was sitting in the garden talking about the day's events. In his inevitable evocation of "returning home," there are some traces of excessive extravagance, but the portraits of the maid Chishavanna, Francesca, and her mad uncle are depicted with great vividness. The last chapter is a recollection of officers and ladies during the Great War, which is another typical Italian scene.

The third book is Alessandro Bonsanti's collection of short stories "La Serue Amorosa," which tells the story of the beginning of the last century, when there was still a Grand Duke in Florence, and when the tutors who taught English to the sons of nobles always inevitably cursed Byron. The stories are either about the lives of bandits in the mountains and forests, or about the experiences of good families. Although there is some rambling, few Italian novels in recent times have been as pleasant to read as this one, because Bonsanti uses a fluent, unpretentious, but never mundane style, and has a remarkable ability to evoke scenes and express personalities. His descriptions of the meeting of two bandit friendships and the life of a Florentine noble family are equally good. He expresses what we might call a picture of life in the age of the horse-drawn carriage, with the leisurely style of an English novelist.

The fourth book is Piero Godpa's "Mozzo." This lovely, short novel, which has previously won the Fiere Letteraria Prize, tells the story of a child born in a small house between La Spezia and Chiavari, on a railway line with many tunnels. Few travelers from La Spezia and Portofino venture deep into this so-called "Five Villages" wilderness, but they are all lovely places, where the people either live by sailing and fishing, or by growing grapes. In this book, Godpa has placed his own deep love for this area of the Ligurian coast.

Mozzo is the protagonist of the book, the son of a railway worker who operates the locomotive's fire. He has a special love for the sea, which even his widowed mother's worries cannot change. His mother sent him to a relative, a priest, in the countryside to be educated, but it was ineffective. Sending him to be an apprentice to a barber was also ineffective. The sea irresistibly called to him. The tone of this pastoral song is one of cheerful simplicity, vividly depicting the bold spirit of an Italian child, especially in the chapter describing Mozzo and several other children rowing the mother of Mocci, her baby, and the family's belongings from Coroneglio to Pieve. A gust of wind arose, and they could not get around the rocky cape, so they ventured into a small bay, where they landed and spent the night with some stonemasons. Throughout the sea voyage, Mozzo was the one who sensitively took command.

The fifth book is Corrado Alvaro's collection of short stories "L'Dmata Alla Finestra."

This is a collection of short stories, mostly reminiscent of the burning landscapes of Calabria and the patriarchal simplicity, with the first one being the best. It describes how a painter painted a portrait of a farm girl and the impact this had on her. The painter finished the painting and left without a second glance, but the girl was infatuated with him and was saddened by it. The book describes this point vividly and colorfully.

The sixth book is Giani Stuparich's collection of short stories "Racconti." The best of these is the last one, a detailed study of a failed life. Antonio Livio, a merchant from Trieste, dies of cancer. Only at the moment of his death does he realize that he has never understood anything, not even the psychology of his own wife.

Recent French Literary Scene

— Cong Ren

Alfred Jolivet

Is a professor of Scandinavian literature and languages at the University of Paris. He obtained a book of Strindberg's letters that had never been published, and used these letters extensively in his book "The Drama of Strindberg." Of the books on Nordic literature published in recent years, this one is undoubtedly the most comprehensive and important. Although Jolivet is a university professor, his book is not one of those introductory books written for students, nor is it a dissertation often done by university professors. In all respects, this book can be said to be a very up-to-date biography of Strindberg. He delves deep into the labyrinth of the Swedish great writer's soul, and in this labyrinth, he proceeds carefully and persistently, sometimes with intuitive insights and due solemnity. Among his many discoveries, one of the most noteworthy is his assertion that Strindberg's mind was feminine, which is to say that Strindberg would not write unless he was stimulated by foreign or external shocks. Strindberg needed a "driving force" to write, and this "driving force" was often found in French literature. Isn't this worth our attention? Therefore, Strindberg under Jolivet's pen has given Jolivet the status of an international critic.

○ ○

There are three books in the "World Tour" (Le Tourdu Monde) series of Glauser: three by Paul Morand, three by Claude Farrère, two by André Maurois, and three by Aaron Jeaul. These books are no better than C. T. Laclaret's "Demi Dieu, ou le VoyageenGrece."

○ ○

Marcel Ayme has published La Table aux Creves Brulebois. He has recently published Un Varien, but unfortunately, this one is not as good as the previous two. This book is only for theologians, and is full of foolish cruelty and vulgar things.

○ ○

Mermoz's Au Lion Tranquille is considered a masterpiece, but his recent work Mal. Loti is far inferior to the previous one. He works in the printing business and is employed by Imprimerie Nationale. He is indeed a true representative of the skilled workers of Paris and is also very proficient in the common language of our time, so everything he writes is of social documentary value.

○ ○

Those who have read Leon Bopp's study of Amie and his novel "The Sin of Alexandre Lenaz" can now read another of his books. The name of this book is "Is He Clever or Stupid?" If we examine it closely, we will not be disappointed. It will still fill our hearts with his original suggestion that people can be explained as a kind of thinking machine.

○ ○

Emile Henriot is the literary news editor of the Times and also a novelist of considerable reputation. A few years ago, his Aricie Brun won the French Academy's Novel Prize. He has recently published "Lost Opportunities" (Occasions Perdues), which is a story of those young French people who were disciples of Barre. These people were wiped out by the war. They were all forthright and uninhibited, with deep thoughts and some romanticism, and opposed their fathers' comfortable hedonism, but they were unprepared for the barbaric struggles (whether moral or material) that lay in wait for those younger than them. Born in the late 1880s and early 1890s, they perished with them. "Lost Opportunities," even if it has no documentary value, is already worth its existence in the two heroines, Jeanne Heylesse and Theuese Aubier.

○ ○

Has everyone heard of Rene Benjamin's "Barres et Joffre"? Many books about Joffre have been published before and after his death. We always thought that there would be no more such books published, but now Benjamin's concise and vigorous "Seven Speeches of the General" has come out. This piece, although only a short forty or so pages, makes the excerpts of those other "Uncle Joffres" retreat. There is also an essay on "Barres," which is longer but extremely vivid and beautiful. Things that come out of Benjamin's pen are originally very good.

○ ○

Andre Lavenson's book "The Sad History of Dostoevsky" is quite noteworthy, because of the many new Russian documents in it that have not yet been translated into French, especially the two volumes of "Letters" in the Moscow National Edition.

○ ○

"Night Flight" (Vol de Nuit) is also a short masterpiece, with a preface by Gide. Antoine de St. Exupery is a famous aviator. This piece is a story that took place one night in the office of the Buenos Aires commercial airline station. It tells how the protagonist, Fabien, was captured, how he was lost in a small cyclone, and how his friend, Reynievier, sacrificed human sorrow to almost inhuman work and duty. This piece is not written very sentimentally, and it uses some technical terms, which makes the tragedy even more tragic.

○ ○

The second volume of "Marcel Proust's Correspondence," by Rupert Pross and Paul Bravet, has now been published by Chez. This volume contains Proust's letters to Mrs. Naryef.

○ ○

Firmin Roz's "From Roosevelt to Hoover" is a well-written and reliable documentary book. Its author has become an authority on American studies by writing this type of book. He often has things published in the "Review of the Old and New Worlds."

○ ○

Among the books related to the colonial exhibition held in Paris in August, we can propose a book by Pierre Mille, Les Fils de L'Ombre et Soliel, which has just been published by Firmin-Didot. Pierre Mille is the founder of French colonial literature. He is the French Kipling and, in a certain sense, also the French Dickens, because once side shadows and caricatures are brought to his pen, they each take on their own lives.

Recent Concerts in Shanghai

— Zhang Ruogu

Previously, the Shanghai Municipal Council Orchestra held symphony concerts every week in the Town Hall on Nanjing Road. From this winter, it has been moved to the Carlton Theatre, with performances starting at 9:00 pm and ending at 11:00 pm every Saturday. Seven concerts have been held this year. Although we don't know what amazing performances will break the record during this music season, except for Heifetz's recent solo violin recital at the New Shanghai Grand Theatre, I personally am very satisfied with the program of last Sunday's concert and have a very good impression.

We should congratulate Mr. Kryger, who directed and conducted the program of that concert, and Mr. Berliulin, the pianist, on their success.

From this concert, we can say that we heard music, truly heard formal music. We were intoxicated by these many beautiful pieces, from Berlioz's "Roman Carnival Overture" to Tchaikovsky's "B-flat minor Serenade," which allowed the audience's souls to be sublimated to the heavenly kingdom of music along with the orchestra's performance.

Mozart's "Musical Joke" is truly a masterpiece. Conductor Kryger truly understood the spirit of the original work. He carefully conducted a group of musicians to fully express the fun of the original piece, and was able to grasp the key points of the original work and analyze various subtle details, which is truly commendable and achieved a glorious success.

As for Grieg's "Peer Gynt Suite," it is a very common work, like a staple food in concerts, so I don't need to be verbose.

Mr. Berliulin is by no means an ordinary piano virtuoso, he is an accomplished artist. His performance of Tchaikovsky's "Serenade" can be taken as a strong guarantee. We hope that his progress will be boundless and that he can maintain his success and glory in art.

Sixth Symphony Concert

In this evening music concert, what made the whole concert more colorful was Mr. Ullstein's solo performance on the Violoncelle. His performance of Saint-Saens' "First Serenade" truly demonstrated his great talent.

Schumann's "Manfred" is a world-famous work. This is a prayer of a lonely hermit in the mountains, a kind of desolate and melancholy tone, which will make sentimental listeners cry.

As for Glazunov's "Waltz," this is a work that is popular in the Yiyuan Garden and several other high-class dance halls. Now it can be heard again in a formal concert hall, which can also be regarded as a creation. The general public is satisfied with this popular dance music. They applaud enthusiastically again and again, but I don't know if they truly understand art and express their appreciation, or if they are just expressing their goodwill to conductor Mr. Foa and all the musicians on the stage.

In the second half of the program, there was Mendelssohn's "Fourth Symphony." Although the conductor worked hard, there was nothing particularly brilliant, and there were many things that could be criticized, but on the whole, this concert gave us considerable satisfaction.

Seventh Symphony Concert

The seventh symphony concert of this year's music season was purely an Italian concert, with the singer being an Italian woman, the conductor being an Italian, and most of the audience being Italian expatriates in Shanghai.

Mrs. Ferrari's singing was one of the most brilliant performances of this evening's concert. The songs she sang were all famous works from operas, such as arias and short songs from "Werther," "La Boheme," and "Madame Butterfly." We can only express our respect for the art of this female artist, but we feel that her voice seems to lack gentleness, and there are perhaps places where she artificially fawns. When she sang sharp sentences, they were a bit irritating to the ears, but on the whole, she is still a first-class famous singer.

Rossini's "Overture from Italy" still achieved great success as always.

After the first half of the program was over, there was a short break, followed by Vittadini's "Nocturnal Harmony" and Santoliquido's "Watercolor."

"Nocturnal Harmony" was publicly performed for the first time in Shanghai, expressing the various sounds of nature very realistically, but it does not seem like an Italian work, but rather seems to be the work of a German musician.

Conductor Ros, the Italian musician, seemed a bit tired this night. He was able to fulfill his duties, and the general audience, especially the Italian expatriates, were satisfied and dispersed.

In the most recent week, there were also several concerts that deserve our attention. The first was the solo recital by Heifetz, the world-famous violin master, and the second was the concert by the China National Conservatory of Music. Unfortunately, I was unable to attend and listen because I was ill and confined to the hospital for many days, so I am unable to express my feelings. I can only report some impressions of the three past symphony concerts. As for my personal loss of missing the Heifetz violin recital, I still consider it a great loss. I hope that those who have heard this world-famous musician perform can write some reports for us.

Shanghai Market

Business News

Yangcheng Restaurant declares that this restaurant is located next to the Qitian Stage at the eastern end of the Great World, and is staffed by famous chefs hired from Guangdong who use pure domestic products to make various tonics, such as Dragon and Tiger Meeting, Three Snake Assembly, Roasted Sea Dog Fish, and Braised Civet Cat, which are especially unique.

The Buddhist Charity Pharmaceutical Factory declares that the Buddhist Charity Pharmaceutical Factory Co., Ltd., initiated by Zheng Pingshu, the former factory director of Shanghai Cuihua Pharmaceutical Factory, and Feng Mingzheng, a disciple of the modern high monk Master Taixu, etc., has raised 100,000 yuan of national currency and has been registered and approved by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government. The factory is located at 164 Tongji Road, Zhabei, and its purpose is to apply science and improve Chinese medicine. It will start work on December 1st, and a lucky day will be chosen for the official opening when Master Taixu, who is lecturing on scriptures in Shaanxi, returns to Shanghai.

Yuanheng Store declares that this store specializes in silk and satin banners, windproof flags and umbrellas, and the low prices and exquisite goods have long been well-known. Now is the first anniversary, in addition to reducing prices and giving away gifts, we will also give away five-corner coupons as a souvenir.

The Mingxing Art Printing Institute at the intersection of Laod Road and Nanjing Road in the British Concession declares that this institute has spent several months of research and specially created famous new and old wedding invitations and various improved receipts and invoices, civilized marriage certificates, stocks, etc., all in dozens of varieties. In order to thank customers, we have made great sacrifices and greatly reduced the prices of various printed materials, and the products are exceptionally fast.

The Jigu Stamp Society at No. 36 Anshen Lane, North Sichuan Road, declares that this society has recently published a book, Chinese Postal Stamp Catalog, which is rich in content and includes illustrations of all types of Chinese postal stamps, as well as detailed notes on the value of Chinese postal stamps. It is a guide for collectors to refer to when purchasing stamps. Each copy sells for six jiao in foreign currency. The Lianghua Advertising Painting Society attached to the society specializes in drawing various advertisements for customers, with low prices and fast delivery. We will also set up three kinds of crash courses in face-to-face and correspondence advertising painting, pattern painting, and photography painting within days, accepting both men and women, and have brochures available. Please send a one-fen stamp for a reply.

The Dingfeng Longan Store at the intersection of Wuma Road and Shilu Road declares that the owner of this store recently went to Xinghua, Fujian and other production areas to purchase a large number of longans with thick flesh, thin shells, and rich nutrition in various varieties, which have now been shipped to Shanghai for customers to choose from. In order to give preferential treatment to patrons, all are sold at flat prices.

The Wanguo Steel Fine Shoe Last Factory declares that the owner of this factory, Mr. Lu Chunjiang, hosted a banquet for the Guangzhou Rubber Industry Inspection Group at Xinghualou the night before last. Those present also included all colleagues from the Shanghai Rubber Products Factory, and Mr. Shi Zhishan, chairman of the Shanghai Public Association Committee, also attended the banquet. After being entertained by Wang Lisan, the director of the Shangjin Society, etc., they visited the factory.

The Fanliyuan Woolen Fabric and Foreign Goods Store at the intersection of Sichuan Road and Beijing Road declares that this store has recently received many new winter goods. Due to the recent gold price relationship, we plan to make huge sacrifices and have an unprecedented big sale for fifteen days from tomorrow to reduce inventory. All goods will be sold at 85% off.
